在以上两种计算情况中, 不论 $\overline{\omega}$ 为何值, 始终取 $\overline{\omega}^{\star} = 0.001$ 和取式(4.170)的一次近似, 即取到 $\overline{\omega}^{\star}$ 的一次项。另外, 通过Sturm-搜索法所得式(4.110)的12个初始特征值 $\overline{\omega}_{(0)}$ 为(其中某些高阶值是人为调整过的)

$$
\left\{ \begin{array}{l l l l} 0. 8 1 2 0 0 E - 7, & 0. 2 2 5 0 0 E - 7, & 0. 1 9 2 3 0 E + 6, & 0. 1 4 5 1 5 E + 7 \\ 0. 5 7 0 1 1 E + 7, & 0. 1 5 3 8 5 E + 8, & 0. 3 5 2 4 3 E + 8, & 0. 7 0 3 6 2 E + 8 \\ 0. 1 2 2 1 3 E + 9, & 0. 2 4 6 1 5 E + 9, & 0. 3 8 2 9 8 E + 9, & 0. 6 1 4 5 5 E + 9 \end{array} \right. \tag {4.176}
$$

表4.2、表4.3中的百分误差分别定义为

$$
\omega \% = \frac {\omega_ {t} - \omega}{\omega_ {t}} \% , \quad \lambda_ {A} \% = \frac {\lambda_ {t} - \lambda_ {A}}{\lambda_ {t}} \% \tag{4.177a}
$$

$$
x \% = \frac {\| x _ {t} - x \| _ {E}}{\| x _ {t} \| _ {E}} \% , \quad \varphi_ {A} \% = \frac {\| \varphi_ {t} - \varphi_ {A} \| _ {E}}{\| \varphi_ {t} \| _ {E}} \% \tag{4.177b}
$$

式中：下标 $t$ 和 $A$ 分别代表试验值和理论值。

由表4.2、表4.3可知：

（1）理想状态(有限元模型无误差)下的结果表明，本节动柔度法在原理上是完全可行的。在同样情况下，其他仅取部件低阶试验模态和高阶模态之部分贡献的方法[2,3]，是无法达到本节动柔度法之精度的。  
(2) 一旦有限元模型出现误差时, 本节动柔度法的精度便明显下降。这说明“动柔度法”对有限元模型之误差较为敏感, 这是它的不足之处。不过, 在有限元模型误差不大时, “动柔度法”仍能综合出足够数量的可用模态参数(表4.3)。一旦有限元模型误差较大时, 就必须求助于模型修正技术, 或对有限元模型进行调整, 这样方可达到工程上所要求的精度, 参考文献[10]便是如此做的, 效果很好。  
（3）本例仅用到各部件的一个弹性模态，却可以综合出整体结构如此多的可用弹性模态，这归功于非线性综合特征方程和“动柔度法”的高精度。  
（4）表4.2中所综合的、可用的第7阶~第10阶频率 $\overline{\omega}$ 和表4.3中可用的第7阶~第8阶频率，都大于部件的最小高阶频率（即第4阶频率） $0.24026\mathrm{E} + 8$ ，这得益于采用了混合移频动柔度式(3.51c)。此时若采用式(3.8c)就不可能达到如此好的精度。  
（5）即使在理想情况下，第11阶频率以后的综合特征对的精度也很差了，这是预料之中的，正如一般特征值问题中的高阶特征对之精度不可信一样。  
(6) 表4.2的理想情况之结果表明, 当本节方法用于理论分析时, 不仅比参考文献[2,3]方法的精度高得多, 甚至可以与参考文献[7-10]之精确方法相匹敌。

# 4.3.4 误差分析与精度改进

无论试验模态基综合技术，还是试验/理论模态基综合技术，都存在一个对其综合结果的误差分析与评估的问题。模综法的精度一般是无法直接验证的，特别是试验模态综合结果更无法由整体结构的试验值来验证。这样就不能确认对某些模态的特殊要求

是否已经满足。这方面的研究甚少，而参考文献[48]对此做了很有益的工作。

设部件的有限元模型已经利用试验模态，通过模型修正技术[32,49]进行修正，且认为修正后的质量矩阵和刚度矩阵已知。然后由修正过的子结构质量矩阵与刚度矩阵组装出整体结构修正模型的质量矩阵 $M$ 与刚度矩阵 $\pmb{K}^{[47]}$ ；由模态综合法给出的近似特征对为 $\lambda_{i}(= \omega_{i}^{2})$ 和 $\pmb{x}_{i}$ ，而假定精确的（未知的）特征对为 $\lambda_{i}'$ 与 $\pmb{x}_{i}'$ 。现就是要分析 $\lambda_{i}$ 和 $\pmb{x}_{i}$ 的误差和可用与否。

# 1. 判断步骤

对于 $\lambda_{i}^{\prime}$ 和 $x_{i}^{\prime}$ , 认为下式精确满足

$$
\left(\boldsymbol {K} - \lambda_ {i} ^ {\prime} \boldsymbol {M}\right) \boldsymbol {x} _ {i} ^ {\prime} \equiv 0 \tag {4.178}
$$

设

$$
\lambda_ {i} ^ {\prime} = \lambda_ {i} + \Delta \lambda_ {i}, \quad x _ {i} ^ {\prime} = x _ {i} + \Delta x _ {i} \tag {4.179}
$$

式中 $\Delta \lambda_{i}$ 与 $\Delta x_{i}$ 为综合特征对的误差项。将式(4.179)代入式(4.178)，并略去1阶以上小量，则有

$$
\left. \left(\boldsymbol {K} - \lambda_ {i} \boldsymbol {M}\right) \boldsymbol {x} _ {i} + \left(\boldsymbol {K} - \lambda_ {i} \boldsymbol {M}\right) \Delta \boldsymbol {x} _ {i} - \Delta \lambda_ {i} \boldsymbol {M} \boldsymbol {x} _ {i} = 0 \right. \tag {4.180}
$$

式中

$$
\left(\boldsymbol {K} - \lambda_ {i} \boldsymbol {M}\right) x _ {i} = f _ {i} \tag {4.181}
$$

就是模态综合过程所产生的误差(力), 它被看作是衡量模态截断误差的一个尺度。若 $\lambda_{i}$ 与 $x_{i}$ 为精确值, 则误差力 $f_{i}$ 的元素在计算误差范围内应该均为零。倘若 $\lambda_{i}$ 和 $x_{i}$ 存在误差, 加上刚度矩阵的元素值又很大, 故 $f_{i}$ 的元素值一般是较大的。据此, 提出下列评估综合模态可用或不可用的判断步骤[48]:

（1）由式(4.181)计算各低阶综合模态的误差力 $f_{i}, i = 1, \dots, s$ 。  
(2) 找出每个 $f_{i}$ 中的最大元素, 且定义它为 $\max f_{i,j}, i = 1, 2, \dots, s; j = 1$ 或 $2 \dots$ 或 $s$ (即最大元素位于 $f_{i}$ 的第 $j$ 行上), 并令其中最小者为常数 $c$ 。

(3) 给定误差限 $\varepsilon \geqslant 1$ , 若 $\max f_{i,j} / c \leqslant \varepsilon$ 则认为是可取模态, 否则是不可取模态。

# 2. 误差分析与精度改进

上述判断步骤仅定性地给出了综合模态可用与否的原则，但对于可用模态参数而言，它们究竟具有多大程度的误差，应该给出定量的分析。为此，将式(4.181)代入式(4.180)，有

$$
\left(\boldsymbol {K} - \lambda_ {i} \boldsymbol {M}\right) \Delta \boldsymbol {x} _ {i} - \Delta \lambda_ {i} \boldsymbol {M} \boldsymbol {x} _ {i} = - \boldsymbol {f} _ {i} \tag {4.182}
$$

另外，由质量归一化条件 $x_{i}^{\prime \mathrm{T}}Mx_{i}^{\prime} = 1$ ，则有

$$
\left(\boldsymbol {x} _ {i} + \Delta \boldsymbol {x} _ {i}\right) ^ {\mathsf {T}} \boldsymbol {M} \left(\boldsymbol {x} _ {i} + \Delta \boldsymbol {x} _ {i}\right) = 1 \tag {4.183}
$$

依靠式(4.182)与式(4.183)，原理上应该能够定量地求解误差项 $\Delta \lambda_{i}$ 和 $\Delta x_{i}$ ，但这样的联立方程求解较繁琐，因此参考文献[48]推荐了一种基于式(4.182)和瑞利商的迭代解法，具体步骤如下：

对于第 $i$ 阶综合特征对 $\lambda_{i}$ 和 $x_{i}$

# 1）初值计算

（1）计算 $f_{i}^{(0)} = (K - \lambda_{i}M)x_{i}$ 。若 $f_{i}^{(0)}$ 较大，转入第(2)步；否则结束，即说明 $\lambda_{i}$ 与 $\pmb{x}_{i}$ 的误差很小，不需要再计算它的 $\Delta \lambda_{i}$ 与 $\Delta x_{i}$

(2) 计算瑞利商 $\lambda_{i}^{(0)}$ :

$$
\lambda_ {i} ^ {(0)} = \frac {\boldsymbol {x} _ {i} ^ {(0) \mathrm {T}} \boldsymbol {K} \boldsymbol {x} _ {i} ^ {(0)}}{\boldsymbol {x} _ {i} ^ {(0) \mathrm {T}} \boldsymbol {M} \boldsymbol {x} _ {i} ^ {(0)}}, \quad \boldsymbol {x} _ {i} ^ {(0)} = \boldsymbol {x} _ {i} \tag {4.184a}
$$

(3) 计算

$$
\Delta \lambda_ {i} ^ {(0)} = \lambda_ {i} ^ {(0)} - \lambda_ {i} \tag {4.184b}
$$

# 2）迭代计算

对于 $p = 0,1,2,\dots$

（4）求解模态误差项 $\Delta x_{i}$

$$
\left(\boldsymbol {K} - \lambda_ {i} ^ {(p)} \boldsymbol {M}\right) \Delta \boldsymbol {x} _ {i} ^ {(p)} = \Delta \lambda_ {i} ^ {(p)} \boldsymbol {M} \boldsymbol {x} _ {i} ^ {(p)} - \boldsymbol {f} _ {i} ^ {(p)} \tag {4.184c}
$$

（5）计算综合特征对的改进值

$$
\boldsymbol {x} _ {i} ^ {(p + 1)} = \boldsymbol {x} _ {i} ^ {(p)} + \Delta \boldsymbol {x} _ {i} ^ {(p)} \tag {4.184d}
$$

$$
\lambda_ {i} ^ {(p + 1)} = \frac {\boldsymbol {x} _ {i} ^ {(p + 1) \mathrm {T}} \boldsymbol {K} \boldsymbol {x} _ {i} ^ {(p + 1)}}{\boldsymbol {x} _ {i} ^ {(p + 1) \mathrm {T}} \boldsymbol {M} \boldsymbol {x} _ {i} ^ {(p + 1)}} \tag {4.184e}
$$

$$
\Delta \lambda_ {i} ^ {(p + 1)} = \lambda_ {i} ^ {(p + 1)} - \lambda_ {i} \tag {4.184f}
$$

(6) 计算

$$
f _ {i} ^ {(p + 1)} = \left(K - \lambda_ {i} ^ {(p + 1)} M\right) x _ {i} ^ {(p + 1)} \tag {4.184g}
$$

(7) 若 $\left| \lambda_{i}^{(p+1)} - \lambda_{i}^{(p)} \right| \leqslant \varepsilon_{1}$ 或 $\left| \max_{j} f_{i,j}^{(p+1)} \right| / \left| \max_{j} f_{i,j}^{(p)} \right| \leqslant \varepsilon_{2}$ , 迭代停止, 从而得误差分析结果: $\Delta \lambda_{i} = \lambda_{i}^{(p+1)} - \lambda_{i}$ 以及 $\Delta x_{i} = x_{i}^{(p+1)} - x_{i}$ ; 否则 $p = : p + 1$ , 且转入第 (4) 步。

以上迭代过程中的 $\varepsilon_{1}$ 与 $\varepsilon_{2}$ 是由精度要求确定的两个小量。由此可知，以上迭代步骤不仅可以定量地给出误差项 $\Delta \lambda_{i}$ 与 $\Delta x_{i}$ ，同时还可以获得精度改善了的综合频率 $\lambda_{i}^{(p + 1)}$ 与模态 $x_{i}^{(p + 1)}$ 。

# 3. 说明

（1）本节推导过程与具体的模综法无关，因此本节方法对所有模综法均适用。另外，模综法也是一种自由度缩聚法，故本节方法也应该可适用于各种缩聚法结果的误差分析。  
（2）本节方法程序简单、计算量小，对于可用模态往往一次迭代便可收敛[48]。  
（3）实际计算时，没有必要生成整体结构的质量矩阵和刚度矩阵，可利用子结构的质量矩阵和刚度矩阵，采用分块相乘的办法执行运算。  
(4) 式(4.184c)之系数矩阵 $(K - \lambda_{i}^{(p)}M)$ 中的 $\lambda_{i}$ 带有“迭代上标” $(p)$ , 这导致每迭代一次, 该系数矩阵就要分解一次, 这样的迭代在工程中是不能接受的。虽然参考文献[48]的数值模拟结果表明: “往往迭代一次便可收敛”, 但这毕竟是一种经验性结论, 因为参考文献[48]并未给出该迭代过程的收敛性证明。为此作者建议: 是否可以将 $(K - \lambda_{i}^{(p)}M)$ 中 $\lambda_{i}$ 的“迭代上标” $(p)$ 改为不变上标 $(o)$ ? 对此, 读者可以权衡考虑。  
(5) 式(4.184)迭代能否具有改善综合模态参数精度的功能完全取决于, 是否获取到一个好的修正模型 $(M, K)$ 。如像参考文

献[47]所做的那样, 由子结构的模态试验结果修正子结构的质量矩阵和刚度矩阵, 然后由这些修正矩阵组装出整体结构的质量矩阵 $\pmb{M}$ 和刚度矩阵 $\pmb{K}$ , 最后求解 $(\pmb{M}, \pmb{K})$ 的特征对, 便得整体结构的所谓“试验子结构模型的综合”模态。好在式(4.184)迭代并不要求能反映任何动力响应特点的 $\pmb{M}$ 和 $\pmb{K}$ , 因此像1.6节指出的, 这样的 $\pmb{M}$ 和 $\pmb{K}$ 由模型修正技术中最简单的矩阵型法获取或按参考文献[47]的方法获取便可。

# 4.4 阻尼结构试验模态综合

阻尼是影响结构动力学特征的一个重要因素, 实际中多数工程结构总是含有阻尼的, 因此在模态综合中采用的无阻尼假设应该不能满足现代工程技术的要求。国、内外学者提出了各种针对阻尼结构的模态综合方法, 其中比较传统的方法是: 首先求解各个子结构的无阻尼振型和频率, 然后组装成整体结构的无阻尼振型和频率, 最后在整体结构的动力学参数中引入假设的模态阻尼。这种方法只能适用于比例阻尼的情况, 并且在阻尼比较大时会带来较大的误差。对于非比例阻尼结构, Hasselman[50]和Craig[51]提出的固定界面方法可用于非比例粘性阻尼结构的模态综合法。Howsman和Craig[52]采用截断的部件复模态与广义实附着模态, 提出自由界面模态综合法, 但计算精度不高。Craig和Ni[53]提出一种阻尼结构的自由界面模态综合法, 定义了“剩余柔度模态”和“状态剩余惯性释放附着模态”并应用到模态综合过程中, 使这一方法获得了较高的精度。Jeffrey和Morgan[54]通过把动力学方程变换到状态空间, 并引入了“约束模态”和“剩余柔度模态”, 提出可用于非比例阻尼结构的模态综合法。W.Wang和J.Kirkhope[55]利用截断的部件复模态, 再以剩余柔度模态和惯性释放模态为补充模态, 提出一种可用于具有刚性和柔性边界结构的自由界面模态综合法。

国内也做了很多这方面的工作。倪振华等[56]针对粘性阻尼

系统提出自由界面模态综合法，并引入了左右投影矩阵，以能够消除系统的刚体模态，同时定义了状态剩余柔度矩阵和状态剩余惯性释放模态，从而将适用于无阻尼系统的 Craig-Chung 方法[61] 成功地推广到粘性阻尼系统。1995年，倪振华[57]针对非对称粘性阻尼结构提出约束部件模态综合法。谭志勇[58]利用实测频响函数分解出阻尼结构的各阶复剩余模态，发展了针对滞后阻尼结构的试验模态综合法。陈国平在参考文献[59]中提出一种新的实空间解耦还原变换方法，通过这种方法可以将非比例粘性阻尼结构的动力学方程变换成解耦的实系数二阶微分方程，在模态空间中保留了模态质量、模态阻尼、模态刚度等物理意义。在此方法的基础上，陈国平[60]提出了基于物理一模态混合变换的模态综合法，能够得到子结构降阶后的质量、刚度和阻尼矩阵，并且综合得到的整体方程仍是时域中的实系数二阶振动方程。

最后指出，阻尼一般分为粘性阻尼与滞后阻尼（亦称结构阻尼）两大类。粘性阻尼假设主要针对结构与外界的相互作用。对于运载火箭与飞机而言，振动阻尼大多数来自其内部结构阻尼，而介质(粘性)阻尼是次要的。

# 4.4.1 滞后阻尼系统[58]

# 1. 动态测试的剩余柔度函数及剩余模态集

设系统由 $\alpha, \beta$ 两个子结构构成，则任意子结构的滞后阻尼运动方程可写成

$$
[ M ] ^ {s} \left\{\ddot {x} \right\} ^ {s} + [ \bar {K} ] ^ {s} \left\{x \right\} ^ {s} = \left\{f \right\} ^ {s} (s = \alpha , \beta) \tag {4.185}
$$

式中： $\overline{K} = K + \mathrm{j}C$ 为复刚度矩阵，而 $K$ 和 $C$ 分别为无阻尼刚度矩阵和结构阻尼矩阵； $\{\pmb{f}\} = \{\pmb{0}, f_{b}^{\mathrm{T}}\}^{\mathrm{T}}, b$ 表示子结构界面自由度分量；以下子结构推导中省略 $s$ ，且设激励外力为 $\{\pmb{f}\} = \{\pmb{f}_{0}\} \mathrm{e}^{j\omega t}, \omega$ 为激励频率， $j = \sqrt{-1}$ 。将式(4.185)的子结构物理坐标位移 $\{x\}$ 转化为模态坐标形式，有

$$
\left| x \right| = \left| x _ {k} + x _ {h} \right| = \left[ \Phi_ {k}, \Phi_ {h} \right] \left\{ \begin{array}{l} q _ {k} \\ q _ {h} \end{array} \right\} = \left[ \Phi \right] \left\{q \right\} \tag {4.186}
$$

其中 $\Phi_k, \Phi_h$ 分别为低阶保留复主模态和高阶复模态，若子结构自由度为 $n$ ，则有 $n_k + n_h = n$ 。对于试验综合过程， $\Phi_k$ 可采用常规测试手段获得，而 $\Phi_h$ 是不可知的，它在自由界面法中采用剩余模态 $\Phi_f$ 来等效。对式(4.186)可写出全部复模态集的归一化正交条件，即

$$
\begin{array}{l} [ \boldsymbol {\Phi} ] ^ {T} [ \bar {\boldsymbol {K}} ] [ \boldsymbol {\Phi} ] = [ \boldsymbol {\Lambda} ] = \operatorname {d i a g} [ \lambda_ {1} ^ {2}, \lambda_ {1} ^ {2}, \dots , \lambda_ {n} ^ {2} ], \\ [ \Phi ] ^ {T} [ M ] [ \Phi ] = [ I ] \tag {4.187} \\ \end{array}
$$

其中 $\lambda_r^2 = (1 + jg_r)\omega_r^2$ 为复特征值， $\omega_r$ 为对应无阻尼条件下的第 $r$ 阶主频， $g_r$ 是 $r$ 阶结构阻尼比。将式(4.186)代入式(4.185)，并利用式(4.187)，得

$$
\left[ \begin{array}{l l} I _ {k} & 0 \\ 0 & I _ {h} \end{array} \right] \left\{ \begin{array}{l} \ddot {\boldsymbol {q}} _ {k} \\ \ddot {\boldsymbol {q}} _ {h} \end{array} \right\} + \left[ \begin{array}{l l} \boldsymbol {A} _ {k} & \boldsymbol {0} \\ 0 & \boldsymbol {A} _ {h} \end{array} \right] \left\{ \begin{array}{l} \boldsymbol {q} _ {k} \\ \boldsymbol {q} _ {h} \end{array} \right\} = \left\{ \begin{array}{l} \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {k} ^ {\mathrm {T}} f \\ \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {k} ^ {\mathrm {T}} f \end{array} \right\} = \left\{ \begin{array}{l l} \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {k b} ^ {\mathrm {T}} & f _ {b} \\ \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {h b} ^ {\mathrm {T}} & f _ {b} \end{array} \right\} \tag {4.188}
$$

由此得到高阶模态坐标 $q_{h}$ 的运动方程为

$$
\boldsymbol {q} _ {h} = \left(\boldsymbol {\Lambda} _ {h} - \omega^ {2} \boldsymbol {I}\right) ^ {- 1} \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {h b} ^ {\mathrm {T}} \boldsymbol {f} _ {b} \tag {4.189}
$$

对应的子结构位移为

$$
x _ {h} = \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {h} \boldsymbol {q} _ {h} = \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {h} \left(\boldsymbol {A} _ {h} - \omega^ {2} \boldsymbol {I}\right) ^ {- 1} \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {h b} ^ {\mathrm {T}} \boldsymbol {f} _ {b} = \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {f} \boldsymbol {f} _ {b} \tag {4.190}
$$

即得到代替高阶模态影响的剩余模态精确表达式为 $\pmb{\Phi}_{f} = \pmb{\Phi}_{h}\left(\pmb{A}_{h} - \omega^{2}\pmb{I}\right)^{-1}\pmb{\Phi}_{hb}^{\mathrm{T}}$ ，对应的模态坐标为界面力。此时 $\pmb{\Phi}_{f}$ 是与 $\omega^{2}$ 相关的不确定值，而该 $\omega^{2}$ 项表示了 $\pmb{\Phi}_{f}$ 中的动力影响分量。如果认为 $\pmb{\Lambda}_{h}\gg \omega^{2}$ ，即动力影响可以忽略不计，则可以将 $\pmb{\Phi}_{f}$ 近似处理为 $\pmb{\Phi}_{h}\pmb{\Lambda}_{h}^{-1}\pmb{\Phi}_{hb}^{\mathrm{T}}$ ，再代入式(4.187），有

$$
\Phi_ {f} \gg \Phi_ {f} ^ {0} = \left(\left[ \bar {K} \right] ^ {- 1} - \Phi_ {k} \Lambda_ {k} ^ {- 1} \Phi_ {k} ^ {\mathrm {T}}\right) \left\{ \begin{array}{l} \mathbf {0} \\ I _ {b} \end{array} \right\} \tag {4.191}
$$

此即经典综合理论采用的简化静刚度下剩余模态近似公式。这里不采用由上式的计算来获取1阶近似剩余模态，而是通过频响函

数实测计算出精确表述的剩余柔度函数离散值，在此基础上从中分解出各阶剩余模态常量。作为频响函数测试方法，剩余柔度函数可以由任意频段的振动试验获得。对于式(4.185)的频响表达式为

$$
H (\omega) = \left\{x \right\} / \left\{f \right\} = 1 / \left(\left[ \bar {K} \right] - \omega^ {2} [ M ]\right) \tag {4.192}
$$

代入正交关系式(4.187)，则得出子结构在界面激励作用下频响函数的模态参数表达式为

$$
\boldsymbol {H} _ {b} (\omega) = \sum_ {i = 1} ^ {n} \frac {\left\{\varphi_ {i} \right| \left\{\varphi_ {i b} \right\} ^ {\mathrm {T}}}{(1 + j g _ {i}) \omega_ {i} ^ {2} - \omega^ {2}} = \sum_ {i = 1} ^ {n} \frac {\left\{\varphi_ {i} \right| \left\{\varphi_ {i b} \right\} ^ {\mathrm {T}}}{\lambda_ {i} ^ {2} - \omega^ {2}} \tag {4.193}
$$

从中减去低阶保留复主模态的影响即得到剩余柔度函数为

$$
\begin{array}{l} \boldsymbol {H} _ {b} ^ {f} (\omega) = \boldsymbol {H} _ {b} (\omega) - \boldsymbol {H} _ {b} ^ {k} (\omega) \\ = \boldsymbol {H} _ {b} (\omega) - \sum_ {i = 1} ^ {k} \frac {\left\{\varphi_ {i} \right\} \left\{\varphi_ {i b} \right\} ^ {\mathrm {T}}}{\left(1 + j g _ {i}\right) \omega_ {i} ^ {2} - \omega^ {2}} \tag {4.194} \\ \end{array}
$$

对比式(4.190)和式(4.194)可知，精确剩余模态 $\Phi_f$ 和剩余柔度函数 $H_b^f (\omega)$ 是一致的，对于悬浮子结构选择 $\omega \neq 0$ 就能避免测试的近似奇异性。以下的工作即是从与 $\omega^2$ 相关的精确剩余模态中分解出各阶近似剩余模态常量，以便进行综合计算。对于 $\Phi_f$ 的精确表达式(4.190)，若条件 $\omega^2\Lambda_k^{-1} < 1$ 成立，则 $\Phi_f$ 可以进行级数分解为

$$
\begin{array}{l} \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {f} = \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {h} \left(\boldsymbol {\Lambda} _ {h} - \omega^ {2} \boldsymbol {I}\right) ^ {- 1} \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {h b} ^ {\mathrm {T}} = \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {h} \boldsymbol {\Lambda} _ {h} ^ {- 1} \left(\boldsymbol {I} - \omega^ {2} \boldsymbol {\Lambda} _ {h} ^ {- 1}\right) ^ {- 1} \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {h b} ^ {\mathrm {T}} \\ = \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {h} \boldsymbol {\Lambda} _ {h} ^ {- 1} \left(\boldsymbol {I} + \sum_ {i = 1} ^ {\infty} \left(\omega^ {2} \boldsymbol {\Lambda} _ {h} ^ {- 1}\right) ^ {i}\right) \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {h b} ^ {\mathrm {T}} \\ = \sum_ {i = 0} ^ {\infty} \omega^ {2 i} \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {h} \boldsymbol {\Lambda} _ {h} ^ {- (i + 1)} \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {h b} ^ {\mathrm {T}} (4.195a) \\ = \sum_ {i = 0} ^ {\infty} \omega^ {2 i} \left(\boldsymbol {\Phi} \boldsymbol {\Lambda} ^ {- (i + 1)} \boldsymbol {\Phi} ^ {\mathrm {T}} - \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {k} \boldsymbol {\Lambda} _ {k} ^ {- (i + 1)} \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {k} ^ {\mathrm {T}}\right) \left\{ \begin{array}{l} 0 \\ I _ {b} \end{array} \right\} (4.195b) \\ \end{array}
$$

此时若仅取 $i = 0$ 即得剩余模态的经典表达式(4.191)。

为了解式(4.195)右端各级数展开项的性质，可将其进行等效变换，对复柔度矩阵 $\pmb {G} = [\overline{\pmb{K}} ]^{-1}$ 分解为保留模态贡献 $G_{k}$ 和高阶模态贡献 $G_{h}$ ，由式(4.187a)可以得出 $\overline{\pmb{K}} = \pmb{\Phi}^{-\mathrm{T}}\pmb {\Lambda}\pmb{\Phi}^{-1}$ ，故有 $\overline{\pmb{K}}^{-1} =$ $\pmb {\varPhi}\pmb{\Lambda}^{-1}\pmb{\Phi}^{\mathrm{T}} = \pmb{\Phi}_{k}\pmb{\Lambda}_{k}^{-1}\pmb{\Phi}_{k}^{\mathrm{T}} + \pmb{\Phi}_{h}\pmb{\Lambda}_{h}^{-1}\pmb{\Phi}_{h}^{\mathrm{T}} = \pmb{G}_{k} + \pmb{G}_{h}$ ，即

$$
\boldsymbol {G} _ {k} = \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {k} \boldsymbol {\Lambda} _ {k} ^ {- 1} \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {k} ^ {\mathrm {T}}, \boldsymbol {G} _ {h} = \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {h} \boldsymbol {\Lambda} _ {h} ^ {- 1} \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {h} ^ {\mathrm {T}}
$$

现分析式(4.195a)中级数的各项：当 $i = 0,1,2,\dots$ 时，该级数的第一、二、三、…项分别为

第一项 $= G_{hb}$

第二项 $= \omega^{2}\Phi_{h}\Lambda_{h}^{-1}\Phi_{h}^{\mathrm{T}}M\Phi_{h}\Lambda_{h}^{-1}\Phi_{hb}^{\mathrm{T}} = \omega^{2}G_{h}MG_{hb}$

第三项 $= \omega^{4}\Phi_{h}\Lambda_{h}^{-1}\Phi_{h}^{\mathrm{T}}M\Phi_{h}\Lambda_{h}^{-1}\Phi_{h}^{\mathrm{T}}M\Phi_{h}\Lambda_{h}^{-1}\Phi_{hb}^{\mathrm{T}} = \omega^{4}G_{h}MG_{h}MG_{hh}$

$$
= \omega^ {4} \left(\boldsymbol {G} _ {h} \boldsymbol {M}\right) ^ {2} \boldsymbol {G} _ {h b}
$$

中 中

由此，可得到精确剩余模态的另一种表达式为

$$
\boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {f} = \sum_ {i = 0} ^ {\infty} \omega^ {2 i} \left(\boldsymbol {G} _ {h} \boldsymbol {M}\right) ^ {i} \boldsymbol {G} _ {h b} \tag {4.196}
$$

由于界面力的偶数阶导数 $f_{b}^{(2i)} (i = 1,2,\dots)$ 与界面力 $f_{b}$ 之间具有关系 $\{f_{b}^{(2i)}\} = (-1)^{i}\omega^{2i}\{f_{b}\}$ , 故 $\{\pmb{x}_k\}$ 可依据式(4.195b)写成

$$
\begin{array}{l} x _ {h} = \Phi_ {f} f _ {b} = \sum_ {i = 0} ^ {\infty} \omega^ {2 i} \left(\Phi \Lambda^ {- (i + 1)} \Phi_ {b} ^ {\mathrm {T}} - \Phi_ {k} \Lambda_ {k} ^ {- (i + 1)} \Phi_ {k b} ^ {\mathrm {T}}\right) f _ {b} \\ = \sum_ {i = 0} ^ {\infty} (- 1) ^ {i} \left(\boldsymbol {\Phi} \boldsymbol {\Lambda} ^ {- (i + 1)} \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {b} ^ {\mathrm {T}} - \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {k} \boldsymbol {\Lambda} _ {k} ^ {- (i + 1)} \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {k b} ^ {\mathrm {T}}\right) \boldsymbol {f} _ {b} ^ {(2 i)} \tag {4.197a} \\ \end{array}
$$

现比较式(4.195b)和式(4.196)便知

$$
\boldsymbol {x} _ {h} = \sum_ {i = 0} ^ {\infty} (- 1) ^ {i} \left(\boldsymbol {G} _ {h} \boldsymbol {M}\right) ^ {i} \boldsymbol {G} _ {h b} f _ {b} ^ {(2 i)} \tag {4.197b}
$$

定义上式中界面力 $2i$ 阶导数的系数项为对应的第 $i$ 阶剩余模态, 可知其物理意义为高阶柔度矩阵 $\pmb{G}_h$ 与质量矩阵 $\pmb{M}$ 的 $i$ 次正交积在界面坐标上的投影, 它在每一测点上的具体值只与结构本

身的固有特性有关, 即仅由 $G_h$ 和 $\pmb{M}$ 所确定。因此可断定, 在 $\pmb{p}$ 点激励 $(p \subset b)$ 条件下任意 $l$ 点的各阶次剩余模态值为常数。若定义 $\left[(\pmb{G}_h\pmb{M})^i\pmb{G}_{hb}\right]_{lp} = \pmb{\Phi}_{flp}^i$ , 称它为第 $i$ 阶近似剩余模态常量。利用式(4.192)和式(4.196), 则有

$$
\boldsymbol {H} _ {l \rho} ^ {f} (\omega) = \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {f l \rho} = \sum_ {i = 0} ^ {\infty} \omega^ {2 i} \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {f l \rho} ^ {i} \tag {4.198}
$$

可以得出结论, 不包含测量误差的剩余柔度函数在子结构保留主模态频率范围内是光滑的多项式函数集合, 它由实部一虚部或幅值一相位角构成, 当取三阶多项式时如图 4.3 所示。因此在试验时, 从剩余柔度函数曲线的光滑性和形状即可大致判断出测试精度, 以及其中包含的高阶剩余模态分量的大小。进一步, 选择光顺性较好的频域段作为可信数据, 由式(4.198)分解得到 $\pmb{\Phi}_{flp}^{i}$ , 它对应于各界面点激励下全部测点的响应组合即构成第 $i$ 阶剩余模态矩阵 $\pmb{\Phi}_{f}^{i}$ 。

从理论上, 剩余模态可分解到任意阶。但仿真计算表明每一高阶值仅为前一阶量级的 $10^{-1} \sim 10^{-3}$ , 因此, 取到 $i = 1 \sim 2$ 就足够了, 设定过高的阶次不仅实测难以准确, 而且使数值计算误差增大。对于每个测点 $l$ 按式(4.198)求取 $\Phi_{flp}^{i}$ 时, 采用离散点下的最小二乘法可减小测试误差。假定选择 $m$ 个不同频率的测点数据, 且取到 $i = 2$ , 对于 $m > i$ , 则由式(4.198)构成一矛盾的线性方程组:

$$
\left\{ \begin{array}{c} H _ {l p} ^ {f} \left(\omega_ {1}\right) \\ \vdots \\ H _ {l p} ^ {f} \left(\omega_ {m}\right) \end{array} \right\} = \left[ \begin{array}{c c c} 1 & \omega_ {1} ^ {2} & \omega_ {1} ^ {4} \\ \vdots & \vdots & \vdots \\ 1 & \omega_ {m} ^ {2} & \omega_ {m} ^ {2} \end{array} \right] \left\{ \begin{array}{c} \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {f l p} ^ {0} \\ \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {f l p} ^ {1} \\ \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {f l p} ^ {2} \end{array} \right\} = [ X ] \left\{ \begin{array}{c} \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {f l p} ^ {0} \\ \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {f l p} ^ {1} \\ \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {f l p} ^ {2} \end{array} \right\} \tag {4.199}
$$

定义目标函数为误差的平方和，进行复数条件下的最小二乘估计，从而解得

$$
\left\{ \begin{array}{l} \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {f l p} ^ {0} \\ \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {f l p} ^ {1} \\ \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {f l p} ^ {2} \end{array} \right\} = \left(\left[ X \right] ^ {\mathrm {T}} [ X ]\right) ^ {- 1} [ X ] ^ {\mathrm {T}} \left\{ \begin{array}{c} \boldsymbol {H} _ {l p} ^ {f} (\omega_ {1}) \\ \vdots \\ \boldsymbol {H} _ {l p} ^ {f} (\omega_ {m}) \end{array} \right\} \tag {4.200}
$$

图片摘要：该图片与韩强国新学\left\{ \begin{array}{l} \boldsymbol {\Phi} {f l p} ^ {0} \\ \boldsymbol {\这部分内容相关。

由于实测时不同频率的数据中包含的误差可能是不相同的，因此可以对不同的测试点加不同的权，构成加权矩阵 $\{W\}$ ，得到加权最小二乘解为

$$
\left\{ \begin{array}{l} \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {f l _ {p}} ^ {0} \\ \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {f l _ {p}} ^ {1} \\ \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {f l _ {p}} ^ {2} \end{array} \right\} = \left(\left[ X \right] ^ {\mathrm {T}} [ W ] [ X ]\right) ^ {- 1} [ X ] ^ {\mathrm {T}} [ W ] \left\{ \begin{array}{c} H _ {l _ {p}} ^ {f} (\omega_ {1}) \\ \vdots \\ H _ {l _ {p}} ^ {f} (\omega_ {m}) \end{array} \right\}
$$

# 2. 自由界面复模态综合方程推导

获得自由界面子结构的保留低价主模态 $\pmb{\Phi}_{k}$ 和剩余模态 $\pmb{\Phi}_{f}$ 之后, 可将式(4.186)重新写成

$$
\left\{x \right\} ^ {s} = \left[ \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {k}, \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {f} \right] ^ {s} \left[ \begin{array}{l} \boldsymbol {q} _ {k} \\ f _ {b} \end{array} \right] ^ {s} = \left[ \boldsymbol {\Phi} \right] ^ {s} \left\{\boldsymbol {p} \right\} ^ {s} \quad (s = \alpha , \beta) \tag {4.202}
$$

根据式(4.198), $\Phi_f$ 为若干阶近似剩余模态常量为系数的 $\omega^2$ 级数, 现以综合时采用 $\Phi_f = \Phi_f^0 + \omega^2\Phi_f^1$ 为例进行推导。将式(4.202)代入式(4.185), 利用模态基的正交关系以及各阶 $\Phi_f^i$ 的定义, 可得

$$
\left[ \begin{array}{l l} I _ {k} & 0 \\ 0 & \mu_ {b} \end{array} \right] ^ {s} \left\{ \begin{array}{l} \ddot {\boldsymbol {q}} _ {k} \\ \ddot {\boldsymbol {f}} _ {b} \end{array} \right\} + \left[ \begin{array}{l l} A _ {k} & 0 \\ 0 & \kappa_ {b} \end{array} \right] ^ {s} \left\{ \begin{array}{l} \boldsymbol {q} _ {k} \\ \boldsymbol {f} _ {b} \end{array} \right\} ^ {s} = \left\{ \begin{array}{l} \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {k b} ^ {\mathrm {T}} f _ {b} \\ \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {f b} ^ {\mathrm {T}} f _ {b} \end{array} \right\} ^ {s} (s = \alpha , \beta) \tag {4.203a}
$$

或简写为

$$
\left[ M (\omega) \right] ^ {s} \left\{\ddot {p} _ {s} \right\} + \left[ K (\omega) \right] ^ {s} \left\{p _ {s} \right\} = \left| F _ {s} (\omega) \right| \quad (s = \alpha , \beta) \tag {4.203b}
$$

式中 $\pmb{\mu}_{b}$ 、 $\kappa_{b}$ 分别称为剩余质量和剩余刚度，即

$$
\boldsymbol {\mu} _ {b} = \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {f} ^ {\mathrm {T}} \boldsymbol {M} \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {f} = \left(\boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {r} ^ {\mathrm {O T}} + \omega^ {2} \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {f} ^ {\mathrm {I T}}\right) \boldsymbol {M} \left(\boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {f} ^ {0} + \omega^ {2} \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {f} ^ {1}\right) =
$$

$$
\Phi_ {f} ^ {0 \mathrm {T}} M \Phi_ {f} ^ {0} + 2 \omega^ {2} \Phi_ {f} ^ {0 \mathrm {T}} M \Phi_ {f} ^ {1} + \omega^ {4} \Phi_ {f} ^ {1 \mathrm {T}} M \Phi_ {f} ^ {1} \tag {4.204a}
$$

同理

$$
\kappa_ {b} = \Phi_ {f} ^ {0 \mathrm {T}} \bar {K} \Phi_ {f} ^ {0} + 2 \omega^ {2} \Phi_ {f} ^ {0 \mathrm {T}} \bar {K} \Phi_ {f} ^ {1} + \omega^ {4} \Phi_ {f} ^ {1 \mathrm {T}} \bar {K} \Phi_ {f} ^ {1} \quad (4. 2 0 4 \mathrm {b})
$$

由定义 $\pmb{\Phi}_{f}^{i} = (\pmb{G}_{h}\pmb{M})^{i}\pmb{G}_{hb}$ ，可知

$$
\boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {f} ^ {0} = \boldsymbol {G} _ {h b} = \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {h} \boldsymbol {\Lambda} _ {h} ^ {- 1} \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {h b} ^ {\mathrm {T}} \tag {4.205a}
$$

$$
\boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {f} ^ {1} = \boldsymbol {G} _ {h} \boldsymbol {M} \boldsymbol {G} _ {h b} \tag {4.205b}
$$

将式(4.205)代入式(4.204），得

$$
\boldsymbol {\mu} _ {b} = \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {f} ^ {\mathrm {T}} \boldsymbol {M} \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {f} = \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {f b} ^ {1} + 2 \omega^ {2} \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {f b} ^ {2} + \omega^ {4} \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {f b} ^ {3} \tag {4.206a}
$$

$$
\kappa_ {b} = \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {f} ^ {\mathrm {T}} \overline {{\boldsymbol {K}}} \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {f} = \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {f b} ^ {0} + 2 \omega^ {2} \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {f b} ^ {1} + \omega^ {4} \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {f b} ^ {2} \tag {4.206b}
$$

式中

$$
\boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {f b} ^ {0} = \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {h b} \boldsymbol {A} _ {h} ^ {- 1} \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {h b} ^ {\mathrm {T}} \tag {4.207}
$$

$$
\boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {f b} ^ {i} = \boldsymbol {G} _ {h b} ^ {\mathrm {T}} \boldsymbol {M} \left(\boldsymbol {G} _ {h} \boldsymbol {M}\right) ^ {i - 1} \boldsymbol {G} _ {h b} \quad (i = 1, 2, \dots) \tag {4.208}
$$

注意：式(4.207)和式(4.208)只是定义式，不是计算式。

若 $\Phi_f$ 仅取到 $\Phi_f^0$ 近似, 则最终综合方程退化为经典理论中的线性特征值问题。现对 $\alpha$ 、 $\beta$ 子结构的式(4.203)根据界面协调条件进行耦合分析。在理想条件下, 有

$$
\boldsymbol {x} _ {b} ^ {\alpha} = \boldsymbol {x} _ {b} ^ {\beta}, \quad f _ {b} ^ {\alpha} = - f _ {b} ^ {\beta} \tag {4.209}
$$

对式(4.209a)，代入位移的具体表达式(4.202)后，得

$$
\begin{array}{l} \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {k b} ^ {\alpha} \boldsymbol {q} _ {k} ^ {\alpha} + \left(\boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {f b} ^ {0 \alpha} + \omega^ {2} \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {f b} ^ {1 \alpha}\right) \boldsymbol {f} _ {b} ^ {\alpha} \\ = \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {k b} ^ {\beta} \boldsymbol {q} _ {k} ^ {\beta} + \left(\boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {f b} ^ {0 \beta}\right) + \omega^ {2} \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {f b} ^ {1 \beta}) \boldsymbol {f} _ {b} ^ {\beta} \tag {4.210} \\ \end{array}
$$

由此解出

$$
\boldsymbol {f} _ {b} ^ {\alpha} = - \boldsymbol {f} _ {b} ^ {\beta} = - A ^ {- 1} \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {k b} ^ {\alpha} \boldsymbol {q} _ {k} ^ {\alpha} + A ^ {- 1} \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {k b} ^ {\beta} \boldsymbol {q} _ {k} ^ {\beta}. \tag {4.211}
$$

式中

$$
A = \left(\Phi_ {f b} ^ {0 \alpha} + \Phi_ {f b} ^ {0 \beta}\right) + \omega^ {2} \left(\Phi_ {f b} ^ {1 \alpha} + \Phi_ {f b} ^ {1 \beta}\right) \tag {4.212}
$$

现将 $\alpha$ 与 $\beta$ 两子结构（部件）的运动方程式(4.203b)堆聚起来：

$$
\left[ \begin{array}{c c} M ^ {\alpha} (\omega) & 0 \\ 0 & M ^ {\beta} (\omega) \end{array} \right] \left\{ \begin{array}{l} \ddot {p} _ {\alpha} \\ \ddots \\ p _ {\beta} \end{array} \right\} + \left[ \begin{array}{c c} K ^ {\alpha} (\omega) & 0 \\ 0 & K ^ {\beta} (\omega) \end{array} \right] \left\{ \begin{array}{l} p _ {\alpha} \\ p _ {\beta} \end{array} \right\} = \left\{ \begin{array}{l} F _ {\alpha} \\ F _ {\beta} \end{array} \right\} \tag {4.213}
$$

另外，由式(4.211)可得模态坐标的协调变换为

$$
\begin{array}{l} \left\{ \begin{array}{l} p _ {\alpha} \\ p _ {\beta} \end{array} \right\} = \left\{ \begin{array}{c} q _ {k} ^ {\alpha} \\ f _ {b} ^ {\alpha} \\ q _ {k} ^ {\beta} \\ f _ {b} ^ {\beta} \end{array} \right\} = \left[ \begin{array}{c c} I _ {k} ^ {\alpha} & 0 \\ - A ^ {- 1} \Phi_ {k b} ^ {\alpha} & A ^ {- 1} \Phi_ {k b} ^ {\beta} \\ 0 & I _ {k} ^ {\beta} \\ A ^ {- 1} \Phi_ {k b} ^ {\alpha} & - A ^ {- 1} \Phi_ {k b} ^ {\beta} \end{array} \right] \left\{ \begin{array}{l} q _ {k} ^ {\alpha} \\ q _ {k} ^ {\beta} \end{array} \right\} \\ = [ \boldsymbol {T} (\omega) ] \{\boldsymbol {\eta} \} \tag {4.214} \\ \end{array}
$$

将式(4.214)代入式(4.213)便得到系统（整体结构）的综合方程为

$$
[ \tilde {M} (\omega) ] \{\ddot {\eta} \} + \{\tilde {K} (\omega) \} \{\eta \} = \{0 \} \tag {4.215}
$$

式中右端项为零可仿照式(4.25)那样证明之，而系数阵分别为

$$
\tilde {\boldsymbol {M}} (\omega) = \left[ \boldsymbol {T} (\omega) \right] ^ {\mathrm {T}} \left[ \begin{array}{c c} \boldsymbol {M} ^ {\alpha} (\omega) & \boldsymbol {0} \\ \boldsymbol {0} & \boldsymbol {M} ^ {\beta} (\omega) \end{array} \right] \left[ \boldsymbol {T} (\omega) \right] \tag {4.216a}
$$

$$
\widetilde {\boldsymbol {K}} (\omega) = \left[ \boldsymbol {T} (\omega) \right] ^ {\mathrm {T}} \left[ \begin{array}{c c} \boldsymbol {K} ^ {\alpha} (\omega) & \boldsymbol {0} \\ \boldsymbol {0} & \boldsymbol {K} ^ {\beta} (\omega) \end{array} \right] \left[ \boldsymbol {T} (\omega) \right] \tag {4.216b}
$$

对于非线性特征方程式(4.215)可采用式(4.112)所示步骤求解。

最后指出，由参考文献[58]的一个典型悬吊梁的实际试验综合结果得知，采用本节方法综合所得整体结构(悬吊梁)的主频尚还可以，而阻尼因子的误差却较大。本节方法属于前述“试验模态基”综合技术。

# 4.4.2 粘性阻尼系统[56]

# 1. 状态空间中的投影矩阵

# 1）一般关系

自由界面部件自由振动方程的状态空间形式可写为

$$
\boldsymbol {A} \dot {\boldsymbol {X}} + \boldsymbol {B} \boldsymbol {X} = \boldsymbol {F} \tag {4.217}
$$

式中

$$
\begin{array}{l} A = \left[ \begin{array}{c c} O & M \\ M & C \end{array} \right], B = \left[ \begin{array}{c c} - M & O \\ O & K \end{array} \right], X = \left[ \begin{array}{c} \dot {x} \\ x \end{array} \right], \\ \boldsymbol {F} = \left[ \begin{array}{l} \boldsymbol {O} \\ \boldsymbol {f} \end{array} \right], \boldsymbol {f} = \left[ \begin{array}{l} \boldsymbol {O} _ {i} \\ \boldsymbol {f} _ {b} \end{array} \right] \tag {4.218} \\ \end{array}
$$

式中： $M,C,K$ 为部件的质量，阻尼，刚度矩阵；部件具有刚体自由度时 $\pmb{K}$ 矩阵奇异；下标 $i,b$ 表示位移向量 $\pmb{x}$ 的内部坐标及界面坐标部分； $f_{b}$ 为来自邻接部件的界面力； $X,F$ 称为状态位移和状态力，当 $M,C,K$ 对称时，存在下列伴随状态方程[52]：

$$
- \boldsymbol {A} ^ {\mathrm {T}} \dot {\boldsymbol {Y}} + \boldsymbol {B} ^ {\mathrm {T}} \boldsymbol {Y} = \boldsymbol {F} ^ {*} \tag {4.219}
$$

式中：伴随状态位移 $Y$ ，伴随状态力 $\pmb{F}^{\star}$ 分别为

$$
\boldsymbol {Y} = \left[ \dot {\boldsymbol {y}} ^ {\mathrm {T}}, \boldsymbol {y} ^ {\mathrm {T}} \right] ^ {\mathrm {T}}, \boldsymbol {F} ^ {*} = \left[ \boldsymbol {O}, \left(\boldsymbol {f} ^ {*}\right) ^ {\mathrm {T}} \right] ^ {\mathrm {T}} \tag {4.220}
$$

式(4.217)与(4.219)的矩阵特征值问题分别为

$$
\boldsymbol {B} \boldsymbol {\Phi} = - \boldsymbol {A} \boldsymbol {\Phi} \boldsymbol {A}, \quad \boldsymbol {\Psi} ^ {\mathrm {T}} \boldsymbol {B} = - \boldsymbol {A} \boldsymbol {\Psi} ^ {\mathrm {T}} \boldsymbol {A} \tag {4.221}
$$

式中： $\pmb{\Phi}$ 和 $\pmb{\Psi}$ 为右和左复模态矩阵， $\pmb{\Lambda}$ 是复谱矩阵。由式(4.221)，有

$$
\overline {{B}} = - \overline {{A}} A = - A \overline {{A}} \tag {4.222}
$$

式中

$$
\overline {{B}} = \boldsymbol {\Psi} ^ {\mathrm {T}} \boldsymbol {B} \boldsymbol {\Phi}, \quad \overline {{A}} = \boldsymbol {\Psi} ^ {\mathrm {T}} \boldsymbol {A} \boldsymbol {\Phi} \tag {4.223}
$$

对于互异的特征值，相应的左、右复模态间有双正交性。

对具有刚体自由度的部件, 复模态矩阵 $\pmb{\Phi}$ 与 $\pmb{\Psi}$ 可分块为

$$
\boldsymbol {\Phi} = \left[ \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {R}, \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {e} \right], \boldsymbol {\Psi} = \left[ \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {R}, \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {e} \right] \tag {4.224}
$$

式中：下标 $R, e$ 表示刚体模态与弹性模态，于是将式(4.224)代入式(4.223)，便得

$$
\overline {{B}} = \operatorname {d i a g} \left[ \overline {{B}} _ {R R}, \overline {{B}} _ {e e} \right], \quad \overline {{A}} = \operatorname {d i a g} \left[ \overline {{A}} _ {R R}, \overline {{A}} _ {e e} \right] \tag {4.225}
$$

式中

$$
\overline {{B}} _ {s s} = \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {s} ^ {\mathrm {T}} \boldsymbol {B} \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {s}, \quad \overline {{A}} _ {s s} = \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {s} ^ {\mathrm {T}} \boldsymbol {A} \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {s}, \quad s = R, e \tag {4.226}
$$

由式(4.223b)可知下列两式：

$$
\boldsymbol {\Phi} ^ {- 1} = \overline {{\boldsymbol {A}}} ^ {- 1} \boldsymbol {\Psi} ^ {\mathrm {T}} \boldsymbol {A} = \left[ \begin{array}{l l} \overline {{\boldsymbol {A}}} _ {R R} ^ {- 1} & \\ & \overline {{\boldsymbol {A}}} _ {e e} ^ {- 1} \end{array} \right] \left[ \begin{array}{l} \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {R} ^ {\mathrm {T}} \\ \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {e} ^ {\mathrm {T}} \end{array} \right] \boldsymbol {A} = \left[ \begin{array}{l} \overline {{\boldsymbol {A}}} _ {R R} ^ {- 1} \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {R} ^ {\mathrm {T}} \boldsymbol {A} \\ \overline {{\boldsymbol {A}}} _ {e e} ^ {- 1} \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {e} ^ {\mathrm {T}} \boldsymbol {A} \end{array} \right] \tag {4.227}
$$

$$
\begin{array}{l} \boldsymbol {\Phi} \boldsymbol {\Phi} ^ {- 1} = \left[ \begin{array}{l} \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {R}, \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {e} \end{array} \right] \left[ \begin{array}{l} \overline {{A}} _ {R R} ^ {- 1} \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {R} ^ {\mathrm {T}} \boldsymbol {A} \\ \overline {{A}} _ {e e} ^ {- 1} \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {e} ^ {\mathrm {T}} \boldsymbol {A} \end{array} \right] \\ = \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {R} \overline {{\boldsymbol {A}}} _ {R R} ^ {- 1} \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {R} ^ {\mathrm {T}} \boldsymbol {A} + \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {e} \overline {{\boldsymbol {A}}} _ {e e} ^ {- 1} \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {e} ^ {\mathrm {T}} \boldsymbol {A} = \boldsymbol {I} \tag {4.228} \\ \end{array}
$$

# 2）投影矩阵

首先定义右投影矩阵 $\pmb{P}$ 为这样一个矩阵：当 $P^{\mathrm{T}}$ 分别左乘于 $\Phi_R$ 与 $\Phi_{e}$ 时， $\Phi_R$ 将消失，而 $\Phi_{e}$ 保持不变，即

$$
P ^ {\mathsf {T}} \left[ \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {R}, \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {e} \right] = \left[ \boldsymbol {O}, \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {e} \right] \tag {4.229}
$$

据此要求来推导 $P^{\mathrm{T}}$ 的具体表达式. 用 $P^{\mathrm{T}}$ 左乘式(4.228)两边，得

$$
P ^ {\mathrm {T}} = P ^ {\mathrm {T}} \Phi_ {R} \bar {A} _ {R R} ^ {- 1} \Psi_ {R} ^ {\mathrm {T}} A + P ^ {\mathrm {T}} \Phi_ {e} \bar {A} _ {e e} ^ {- 1} \Psi_ {e} ^ {\mathrm {T}} A = \Phi_ {e} \bar {A} _ {e e} ^ {- 1} \Psi_ {e} ^ {\mathrm {T}} A \tag {4.230}
$$

再利用式(4.228)，由上式可得 $P^{\mathrm{T}}$ 的具体表达式为

$$
\boldsymbol {P} ^ {\mathrm {T}} = \boldsymbol {I} - \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {R} \overline {{\boldsymbol {A}}} _ {R R} ^ {- 1} \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {R} ^ {\mathrm {T}} \boldsymbol {A} \tag {4.231}
$$

其次，定义左投影矩阵 $Q$ 为

$$
Q ^ {\mathrm {T}} \left[ \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {R}, \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {e} \right] = \left[ \boldsymbol {O}, \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {e} \right] \tag {4.232}
$$

由式(4.228)，知

$$
A ^ {- 1} = \Phi_ {R} \bar {A} _ {R R} ^ {- 1} \Psi_ {R} ^ {\mathrm {T}} + \Phi_ {e} \bar {A} _ {e e} ^ {- 1} \Psi_ {e} ^ {\mathrm {T}}
$$

则有

$$
A ^ {- 1} Q = \Phi_ {R} \bar {A} _ {R R} ^ {- 1} \Psi_ {R} ^ {\mathrm {T}} Q + \Phi_ {e} \bar {A} _ {e e} ^ {- 1} \Psi_ {e} ^ {\mathrm {T}} Q = \Phi_ {e} \bar {A} _ {e e} ^ {- 1} \Psi_ {e} ^ {\mathrm {T}}
$$

即得

$$
Q = A \Phi_ {e} \bar {A} _ {e e} ^ {- 1} \Psi_ {e} ^ {\mathrm {T}} \tag {4.233}
$$

由式(4.223b)，知

$$
\boldsymbol {\Psi} ^ {- T} = \boldsymbol {A} \Phi \overline {{\boldsymbol {A}}} ^ {- 1}
$$

于是有

$$
\begin{array}{l} \boldsymbol {\Psi} ^ {- \mathrm {T}} \boldsymbol {\Psi} ^ {\mathrm {T}} = \boldsymbol {A} \left[ \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {R}, \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {e} \right] \left[ \begin{array}{c c} \bar {\boldsymbol {A}} _ {R R} ^ {- 1} & \boldsymbol {O} \\ \boldsymbol {O} & \bar {\boldsymbol {A}} _ {e e} ^ {- 1} \end{array} \right] \left[ \begin{array}{l} \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {R} ^ {\mathrm {T}} \\ \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {e} ^ {\mathrm {T}} \end{array} \right] = \\ A \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {R} \overline {{\boldsymbol {A}}} _ {R R} ^ {- 1} \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {R} ^ {\mathrm {T}} + A \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {e} \overline {{\boldsymbol {A}}} _ {e e} ^ {- 1} \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {e} ^ {\mathrm {T}} = I \tag {4.234} \\ \end{array}
$$

最后由式(4.233)和(4.234)得到 $Q$ 的具体表达式为

$$
Q = I - A \Phi_ {R} \overline {{A}} _ {R R} ^ {- 1} \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {R} ^ {\dagger} \tag {4.235}
$$

由定义知 $P$ 和 $Q$ 都是等幂矩阵（即 $PP \cdots P = P$ 和 $QQ \cdots Q = Q$ 等）。另外，由式(4.231)和(4.235)，易知有下列关系：

$$
\begin{array}{l} Q A = A P ^ {\mathrm {T}} (4.236) \\ P ^ {\top} \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {R} = Q ^ {\top} \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {R} = 0, P ^ {\top} \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {e} = \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {e}, Q ^ {\top} \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {e} = \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {e} (4.237) \\ \end{array}
$$

3）投影矩阵对状态位移的算子作用

设状态位移 $X$ 包含有刚体位移 $X_{R}$ ，则 $X$ 可按右模态展开为

$$
X = X _ {R} + X _ {e} = \Phi_ {R} \eta_ {R} + \Phi_ {e} \eta_ {e} \tag {4.238}
$$

于是有

$$
\boldsymbol {P} ^ {\mathrm {T}} \boldsymbol {X} = \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {e} \boldsymbol {\eta} _ {e} = \boldsymbol {X} - \boldsymbol {X} _ {R} \tag {4.239}
$$

这说明 $P^{\mathrm{T}}$ 左乘于任意状态位移时，便可以消除其中的刚体位移成分。同样有

$$
Q ^ {\mathrm {T}} Y = Y - Y _ {R} \tag {4.240}
$$

现将复谱矩阵 $\pmb{A}$ 按式(4.225），分块为

$$
\Lambda = \operatorname {d i a g} \left[ \Lambda_ {R R}, \Lambda_ {e e} \right] \tag {4.241}
$$

将式(4.241)和(4.224a)代入式(4.221a)，有

$$
B \left[ \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {R}, \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {e} \right] = - A \left[ \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {R}, \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {e} \right] \left[ \begin{array}{l l} \boldsymbol {\Lambda} _ {R R} & \\ & \boldsymbol {\Lambda} _ {e e} \end{array} \right]
$$

即

$$
\left[ B \Phi_ {R}, B \Phi_ {e} \right] = \left[ - A \Phi_ {R} \Lambda_ {R R}, - A \Phi_ {e} \Lambda_ {e e} \right]
$$

故有

$$
\boldsymbol {B} \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {R} = - \boldsymbol {A} \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {R} \boldsymbol {\Lambda} _ {R R} \tag {4.242}
$$

同样，将式(4.241)和(4.224b)代入式(4.221b)，则有

$$
\boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {R} ^ {T} \boldsymbol {B} = - \boldsymbol {\Lambda} _ {R R} \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {R} ^ {T} \boldsymbol {A} \tag {4.243}
$$

# 4）投影矩阵对状态力的算子作用

现分两种情况证明这种算子作用。

# （1）部件零频特征子空间不亏损

设部件刚体自由度数为 $n_R$ ，零特征值是式（4.221）的 $n_R$ 重根，这时部件有 $n_R$ 个常规右与左状态刚体模态，可构造为[52]

$$
\boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {R} = \left[ \left(\boldsymbol {O} ^ {V}\right) ^ {T}, \left(\boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {R} ^ {D}\right) ^ {T} \right] ^ {T}, \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {R} = \left[ \left(\boldsymbol {O} ^ {V}\right) ^ {T}, \left(\boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {R} ^ {D}\right) ^ {T} \right] ^ {T} \tag {4.244}
$$

式中：上标 $V, D$ 表示状态向量中的速度及位移部分； $\Phi_R^D, \Psi_R^D$ 分别来自于下列方程：

$$
\boldsymbol {k} \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {R} ^ {D} = \boldsymbol {0}, \quad \boldsymbol {k} \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {R} ^ {D} = \boldsymbol {0} \tag {4.245}
$$

由式(4.218)、式(4.242)、式(4.243)及式(4.245)，易知

$$
\boldsymbol {B} \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {R} = \boldsymbol {O}, \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {R} ^ {\mathrm {T}} \boldsymbol {B} = \boldsymbol {O}, \boldsymbol {\Lambda} _ {R R} = \boldsymbol {O} \tag {4.246}
$$

于是由式(4.231)和式(4.235)以及利用式(4.246)容易证明下列关系：

$$
Q B = B P ^ {\intercal} \tag {4.247}
$$

若对式(4.217)的状态力 $\pmb{F}$ 左乘 $\pmb{Q}$ , 由式(4.236)、式(4.247)及式(4.239)得

$$
\begin{array}{l} Q F = Q (A \dot {X} + B X) = A P ^ {\top} \dot {X} + B P ^ {\top} X \\ = A \left(\dot {X} - \dot {X} _ {R}\right) + B \left(X - X _ {R}\right) = F - \left(A \dot {X} _ {R} + B X _ {R}\right) \\ = \left[ \begin{array}{l} \boldsymbol {O} \\ f \end{array} \right] - \left(\left[ \begin{array}{l l} \boldsymbol {O} & \boldsymbol {M} \\ \boldsymbol {M} & \boldsymbol {C} \end{array} \right] \left[ \begin{array}{l} \ddot {\boldsymbol {x}} _ {R} \\ \dot {\boldsymbol {x}} _ {R} \end{array} \right] + \left[ \begin{array}{l l} - \boldsymbol {M} & \boldsymbol {O} \\ \boldsymbol {O} & \boldsymbol {K} \end{array} \right] \left[ \begin{array}{l} \dot {\boldsymbol {x}} _ {R} \\ \boldsymbol {x} _ {R} \end{array} \right]\right) \\ = \left\{ \begin{array}{l} \boldsymbol {O} \\ f \end{array} \right\} - \left(\left[ \begin{array}{c} \boldsymbol {M} \dot {\boldsymbol {x}} _ {R} \\ \boldsymbol {M} \ddot {\boldsymbol {x}} _ {R} + \boldsymbol {C} \dot {\boldsymbol {x}} _ {R} \end{array} \right] + \left[ \begin{array}{c} - \boldsymbol {M} \dot {\boldsymbol {x}} _ {R} \\ \boldsymbol {K} \boldsymbol {x} _ {R} \end{array} \right]\right) \\ = \left[ \begin{array}{c} O \\ f - M \ddot {x} _ {R} - C \dot {x} _ {R} \end{array} \right] \tag {4.248} \\ \end{array}
$$

可见，作用于悬浮部件的力 $f$ 变为被刚体运动引起的惯性力和阻尼力所平衡的力，简称为自平衡力。

# （2）部件零频特征子空间亏损

此时零特征值是式(4.221)的 $2n_{R}$ 重根，这时部件除有 $n_{R}$ 个常规右刚体模态（记为 $\pmb{\Phi}_{R}^{\prime}$ ）之外，还有 $n_{R}$ 个相应的广义右刚体模态，记为 $\pmb{\Phi}_{R}^{\prime \prime}$ 。 $\pmb{\Phi}_{R}^{\prime}$ 和 $\pmb{\Phi}_{R}^{\prime \prime}$ 的关系为[62]

$$
\left(- \boldsymbol {A} ^ {- 1} \boldsymbol {B}\right) \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {R} ^ {\prime \prime} = \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {R} ^ {\prime} \tag {4.249}
$$

由式（4.249），知

$$
- B \Phi_ {R} ^ {\prime \prime} = A \Phi_ {R} ^ {\prime}
$$

即

$$
- \left[ \begin{array}{c c} - M & O \\ O & K \end{array} \right] \left[ \begin{array}{l} \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {R} ^ {\prime V} \\ \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {R} ^ {\prime D} \end{array} \right] = \left[ \begin{array}{c c} O & M \\ M & C \end{array} \right] \left[ \begin{array}{l} \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {R} ^ {\prime V} \\ \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {R} ^ {\prime D} \end{array} \right]
$$

即

$$
\left[ \begin{array}{c} \boldsymbol {M} \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {R} ^ {\prime V} \\ - \boldsymbol {K} \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {R} ^ {\prime D} \end{array} \right] = \left[ \begin{array}{c} \boldsymbol {M} \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {R} ^ {\prime D} \\ \boldsymbol {M} \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {R} ^ {\prime V} + \boldsymbol {C} \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {R} ^ {\prime D} \end{array} \right] \tag {4.250}
$$

实际上 $\pmb{\Phi}_{R}^{\prime} = \pmb{\Phi}_{R}$ ，故 $\pmb{\Phi}_{R}^{\prime V} = \pmb{\Phi}_{R}^{V} = \pmb{0}$ （见式（4.244））。将此两等式引

人式(4.250)便得到

$$
\boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {R} ^ {\prime \prime V} = \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {R} ^ {D}, \boldsymbol {k} \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {R} ^ {\prime \prime D} = - \boldsymbol {c} \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {R} ^ {D} \tag {4.251}
$$

式(4.251)就是 $\Phi_R''$ 的速度部分 $\Phi_R^{\prime \prime V}$ 及位移部分 $\Phi_R^{\prime \prime D}$ 需满足的关系。因 $k$ 矩阵奇异，式(4.251)第二式仅对某些半正定阻尼矩阵有解，这时有

$$
c \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {R} ^ {D} = \boldsymbol {0} \tag {4.252}
$$

为简单可取 $\pmb{\Phi}_{R}^{\prime \prime D} = \pmb{0}$ ，于是再利用式(4.251a)可知完备的状态右刚体模态为

$$
\boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {R} = \left[ \begin{array}{l l} \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {R} ^ {\prime}, & \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {R} ^ {\prime \prime} \end{array} \right] = \left[ \begin{array}{c c} \boldsymbol {O} & \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {R} ^ {D} \\ \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {R} ^ {D} & \boldsymbol {O} \end{array} \right] \tag {4.253}
$$

状态左刚体模态形如上式，只是 $\Phi_R^D$ 改为 $\Psi_{R}^{D}$ 。由式(4.226b）和式（4.253），知

$$
\begin{array}{l} \overline {{A}} _ {R R} = \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {R} ^ {\mathrm {T}} \boldsymbol {A} \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {R} = \left[ \begin{array}{c c} O & \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {R} ^ {D} \\ \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {R} ^ {D} & O \end{array} \right] \left[ \begin{array}{c c} O & M \\ M & C \end{array} \right] \left[ \begin{array}{c c} O & \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {R} ^ {D} \\ \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {R} ^ {D} & O \end{array} \right] \\ = \left[ \begin{array}{c c} \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {R} ^ {D} C \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {R} ^ {D} & \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {R} ^ {D} M \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {R} ^ {D} \\ \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {R} ^ {D} M \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {R} ^ {D} & 0 \end{array} \right] = \left[ \begin{array}{c c} 0 & \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {R} ^ {D} M \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {R} ^ {D} \\ \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {R} ^ {D} M \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {R} ^ {D} & 0 \end{array} \right] \\ \end{array}
$$

于是有

$$
\overline {{A}} _ {R R} ^ {- 1} = \left[ \begin{array}{c c} O & \left(\Psi_ {R} ^ {D} M \Phi_ {R} ^ {D}\right) ^ {- 1} \\ \left(\Psi_ {R} ^ {D} M \Phi_ {R} ^ {D}\right) ^ {- 1} & O \end{array} \right] \tag {4.254}
$$

同样，由式(4.226a)和(4.253)，可求得（利用式(4.245))

$$
\overline {{B}} _ {R R} = \left[ \begin{array}{c c} O & O \\ O & - \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {R} ^ {D} M \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {R} ^ {D} \end{array} \right] \tag {4.255}
$$

由式(4.222)，易知

$$
\boldsymbol {A} _ {R R} = - \overline {{\boldsymbol {A}}} _ {R R} ^ {- 1} \overline {{\boldsymbol {B}}} _ {R R} =
$$

$$
\begin{array}{l} - \left[ \begin{array}{c c} O & \left(\Psi_ {R} ^ {D} M \Phi_ {R} ^ {D}\right) ^ {- 1} \\ \left(\Psi_ {R} ^ {D} M \Phi_ {R} ^ {D}\right) ^ {- 1} & O \end{array} \right] \left[ \begin{array}{c c} O & O \\ O & - \Psi_ {R} ^ {D} M \Phi_ {R} ^ {D} \end{array} \right] \\ = \left[ \begin{array}{l l} O _ {R R} & I _ {R R} \\ O _ {R R} & O _ {R R} \end{array} \right] \tag {4.256} \\ \end{array}
$$

再由式(4.242)和式(4.243)，分别得知

$$
\boldsymbol {B} \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {R} ^ {\prime} = \boldsymbol {0}, \boldsymbol {B} \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {R} ^ {\prime \prime} = - \boldsymbol {A} \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {R} ^ {\prime} \tag {4.257a}
$$

和

$$
\boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {R} ^ {\prime \mathrm {T}} \boldsymbol {B} = - \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {R} ^ {\prime \mathrm {T}} \boldsymbol {A}, \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {R} ^ {\prime \mathrm {T}} \boldsymbol {B} = 0 \tag {4.257b}
$$

最后由式(4.235)及式(4.257)，可得

$$
\begin{array}{l} Q B = \left(I - A \left[ \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {R} ^ {\prime}, \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {R} ^ {\prime \prime} \right] \bar {A} _ {R R} ^ {- 1} \left[ \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {R} ^ {\prime}, \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {R} ^ {\prime \prime} \right] ^ {\mathrm {T}}\right) \boldsymbol {B} \\ = \boldsymbol {B} - \left(A \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {R} ^ {\prime}\right) \bar {\boldsymbol {A}} _ {R R} ^ {- 1} \left(\boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {R} ^ {\prime \mathrm {T}} \boldsymbol {B}\right) - A \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {R} ^ {\prime \prime} \bar {\boldsymbol {A}} _ {R R} ^ {- 1} \left(\boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {R} ^ {\prime \mathrm {T}} \boldsymbol {B}\right) \\ = \boldsymbol {B} - \boldsymbol {B} \Phi_ {R} ^ {\prime \prime} \overline {{\boldsymbol {A}}} _ {R R} ^ {- 1} \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {R} ^ {\prime \prime T} \boldsymbol {A} \tag {4.258} \\ \end{array}
$$

由于 $B\Phi_{R}^{\prime} = 0$ （见式（4.257a）），故可以在式(4.258)的右端配上一项 $\pmb{B}\pmb{\Phi}_{R}^{\prime}\overline{\pmb{A}}_{RR}^{-1}\pmb{\Psi}_{R}^{\prime T}\pmb{A}(= \pmb {O})$ ，即得

$$
\begin{array}{l} Q B = B - B \Phi_ {R} ^ {\prime} \bar {A} _ {R R} ^ {- 1} \Psi_ {R} ^ {\prime \top} A - B \Phi_ {R} ^ {\prime \prime} \bar {A} _ {R R} ^ {- 1} \Psi_ {R} ^ {\prime \prime \top} A \\ = B \left(I - \Phi_ {R} ^ {\prime} \bar {A} _ {R R} ^ {- 1} \Psi_ {R} ^ {\prime T} A - \Phi_ {R} ^ {\prime \prime} \bar {A} _ {R R} ^ {- 1} \Psi_ {R} ^ {\prime \prime T} A\right) \\ = B \left(I - \left[ \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {R} ^ {\prime}, \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {R} ^ {\prime \prime} \right] \bar {A} _ {R R} ^ {- 1} \left[ \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {R} ^ {\prime}, \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {R} ^ {\prime \prime} \right] ^ {\top} \boldsymbol {A}\right) \\ = \boldsymbol {B} (\boldsymbol {I} - \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {R} \overline {{\boldsymbol {A}}} _ {R R} ^ {- 1} \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {R} ^ {\top} \boldsymbol {A}) \\ = \boldsymbol {B} \boldsymbol {P} ^ {\mathrm {T}} \tag {4.259} \\ \end{array}
$$

即式(4.247)仍然成立。这样，式(4.248)表达的算子作用仍然成立。

# 2. 状态剩余模态

若定义下列状态单位界面力矩阵：

$$
\boldsymbol {F} _ {a} = \left[ \boldsymbol {O} _ {b i}, \boldsymbol {O} _ {b b}, \boldsymbol {O} _ {b i}, I _ {b b} \right] ^ {\intercal} \tag {4.260}
$$

由式(4.248)知， $QF_{a}$ 即为自平衡状态单位界面力。设矩阵 $\hat{\Phi}_{a}$ 的各列是部件受 $QF_{a}$ 作用并在人为定义的刚体自由度有静定约束而产生的状态静位移，即

$$
B \hat {\Phi} _ {a} = Q F _ {a} \tag {4.261}
$$

由此解出

$$
\hat {\boldsymbol {\Phi}} _ {a} = D Q F _ {a} \tag {4.262}
$$

式中

$$
\boldsymbol {D} = \operatorname {d i a g} \left[ - \boldsymbol {M} ^ {- 1}, \boldsymbol {K} _ {I I} ^ {- 1}, \boldsymbol {O} _ {R R} \right] \tag {4.263}
$$

其中 $K_{ll}$ 是 $\pmb{K}$ 的一个主子矩阵， $l$ 表示内部坐标与赘余界面坐标的总和，并约定刚体坐标位于位移向量的最后部分。为消除右刚体模态，将(4.262)左乘 $\pmb{P}^{\mathrm{T}}$ ，便得到下列与 $\Psi_R$ 正交的状态惯性释放附着模态：

$$
\boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {a} = \left(\boldsymbol {P} ^ {\mathrm {T}} \boldsymbol {D} \boldsymbol {Q}\right) \boldsymbol {F} _ {a} = \boldsymbol {D} _ {c} \boldsymbol {F} _ {a} \tag {4.264}
$$

式中： $D_{e} = P^{\mathrm{T}}DQ$ 为状态弹性柔度矩阵。

现在可将 $\Phi_{a}$ 按右弹性复模态展开为 $\Phi_{a} = \Phi_{e}E$ ，显然 $\Phi_{a}$ 也满足式(4.261)，因此将 $\Phi_{a} = \Phi_{e}E$ 代入式(4.261），且左乘 $\Psi_{e}^{\mathrm{T}}$ ，有

$$
\boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {e} ^ {\mathrm {T}} \boldsymbol {B} \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {e} \boldsymbol {E} = \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {e} ^ {\mathrm {T}} \boldsymbol {Q} \boldsymbol {F} _ {o}
$$

即得

$$
E = \bar {B} _ {e e} ^ {- 1} \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {e} ^ {\mathrm {T}} Q F _ {a} = \bar {B} _ {e e} ^ {- 1} \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {e} ^ {\mathrm {T}} F _ {a} \tag {4.265}
$$

于是

$$
\boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {a} = \left(\boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {e} \overline {{\boldsymbol {B}}} _ {e e} ^ {- 1} \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {e} ^ {\mathrm {T}}\right) \boldsymbol {F} _ {a} \tag {4.266}
$$

比较上式与(4.264)得知，括号内部分表示同一个部件的状态弹性柔度矩阵，故有

$$
D _ {e} = P ^ {\mathrm {T}} D Q = \Phi_ {e} \bar {B} _ {e e} ^ {- 1} \Psi_ {e} ^ {\mathrm {T}} \tag {4.267}
$$

若将弹性复模态分块为

$$
\boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {e} = \left[ \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {p}, \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {h} \right], \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {e} = \left[ \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {p}, \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {h} \right] \tag {4.268}
$$

式中：下标 $p, h$ 表示保留模态部分与删除(高阶)模态部分，则

$$
D _ {e} = D _ {p} + D _ {h} \tag {4.269}
$$

式中

$$
\boldsymbol {D} _ {p} = \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {p} \overline {{\boldsymbol {B}}} _ {p p} ^ {- 1} \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {p} ^ {\mathrm {T}}, \boldsymbol {D} _ {h} = \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {h} \overline {{\boldsymbol {B}}} _ {h h} ^ {- 1} \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {h} ^ {\mathrm {T}}, \overline {{\boldsymbol {B}}} _ {s s} = \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {s} ^ {\mathrm {T}} \boldsymbol {B} \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {s} (s = p, h) \tag {4.270}
$$

式中： $D_{h}$ 为状态剩余弹性柔度矩阵，它无需高阶模态，可由下式求得，即

$$
\boldsymbol {D} _ {h} = \boldsymbol {P} ^ {\mathrm {T}} \boldsymbol {D} \boldsymbol {Q} - \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {p} \overline {{\boldsymbol {B}}} _ {p p} ^ {- 1} \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {p} ^ {\mathrm {T}} \tag {4.271}
$$

对于无刚体自由度的部件不难得知

$$
\boldsymbol {P} = \boldsymbol {Q} = \boldsymbol {I}, \quad \boldsymbol {D} _ {\dot {n}} = \boldsymbol {B} ^ {- 1} - \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {p} \overline {{\boldsymbol {B}}} _ {p p} ^ {- 1} \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {p} ^ {\mathrm {T}} \tag {4.272}
$$

# 1）右状态剩余模态

类似式(4.264)，定义右状态剩余（惯性释放附着）模态为

$$
\boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {d} = \boldsymbol {D} _ {h} \boldsymbol {F} _ {a} \tag {4.273}
$$

由式(4.270)知 $\Phi_d$ 实际是高阶弹性模态的线性组合, 故与 $\Psi_R, \Psi_p$ 邦正交, 若将 $\Phi_d$ 分块为

$$
\boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {d} = \left[ \left(\boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {i d} ^ {V}\right) ^ {T}, \left(\boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {b d} ^ {V}\right) ^ {T}, \left(\boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {i d} ^ {D}\right) ^ {T}, \left(\boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {b d} ^ {D}\right) ^ {T} \right] ^ {T} \tag {4.274}
$$

$\pmb{\Phi}_{h}, \pmb{\Psi}_{h}, \pmb{D}_{h}$ 也做相应分块, 则由式 (4.260)、式 (4.270b)、式 (4.273), 得

$$
\begin{array}{l} \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {d} = \left\{ \begin{array}{l} \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {i d} ^ {V} \\ \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {b d} ^ {V} \\ \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {i d} ^ {D} \\ \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {b d} ^ {D} \end{array} \right] = \left[ \begin{array}{l} \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {i h} ^ {V} \\ \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {b h} ^ {V} \\ \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {i h} ^ {D} \\ \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {b h} ^ {D} \end{array} \right] \overline {{\boldsymbol {B}}} _ {h h} ^ {- 1} \left[ \begin{array}{l l l l l} \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {i h} ^ {V T}, & \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {b h} ^ {V T}, & \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {i h} ^ {D T}, & \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {b h} ^ {D T} \end{array} \right] \left[ \begin{array}{l} \boldsymbol {O} _ {b i} \\ \boldsymbol {O} _ {b b} \\ \boldsymbol {O} _ {b i} \\ \boldsymbol {I} _ {b b} \end{array} \right] \\ = \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {h} \overline {{\boldsymbol {B}}} _ {h h} ^ {- 1} \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {b h} ^ {D T} \tag {4.275a} \\ \end{array}
$$

人式(4.275a），还可看出

$$
\boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {b d} ^ {D} = \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {b h} ^ {D} \overline {{\boldsymbol {B}}} _ {b h} ^ {- 1} \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {b h} ^ {D T} = \left(\boldsymbol {D} _ {h}\right) _ {b b} ^ {D D} \tag {4.275b}
$$

可见 $\pmb{\Phi}_{d}$ 的位移界面部分 $\pmb{\Phi}_{bd}^{D}$ 正是 $\pmb{D}_{h}$ 的位移界面部分。

# 2）左状态剩余模态

定义左状态剩余模态 $\Psi_{d}$ 为

$$
\boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {d} = \boldsymbol {D} _ {h} ^ {\mathrm {T}} \boldsymbol {F} _ {a} \tag {4.276}
$$

相应于式(4.275)，有

$$
\boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {d} = \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {h} \left(\bar {\boldsymbol {B}} _ {h h} ^ {- 1}\right) ^ {\mathrm {T}} \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {b h} ^ {D T} \tag {4.277a}
$$

$$
\boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {b d} ^ {D} = \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {b h} ^ {D} \left(\overline {{\boldsymbol {B}}} _ {h h} ^ {- 1}\right) ^ {\mathrm {T}} \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {b h} ^ {D \mathrm {T}} = \left[ \left(\boldsymbol {D} _ {h}\right) _ {b b} ^ {D D} \right] ^ {\mathrm {T}} \tag {4.277b}
$$

比较式(4.275b)和式(4.277b)，知

$$
\boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {b d} ^ {D} = \left(\boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {b d} ^ {D}\right) ^ {\mathrm {T}} \tag {4.278}
$$

# 3. 部件(子结构)广义运动方程

现设部件的模态矩阵 $\pmb{U}$ 和 $\pmb{V}$ 分别为

$$
\boldsymbol {U} = \left[ \begin{array}{l} \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {R}, \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {p}, \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {d} \end{array} \right] = \left[ \begin{array}{l} \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {k}, \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {d} \end{array} \right],
$$

$$
\boldsymbol {V} = \left[ \begin{array}{l} \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {R}, \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {p}, \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {d} \end{array} \right] = \left[ \begin{array}{l} \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {k}, \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {d} \end{array} \right] \tag {4.279}
$$

对式(4.217)作下列坐标变换：

$$
X = U \boldsymbol {\eta} = \left[ \begin{array}{l} \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {k}, \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {d} \end{array} \right] \left[ \begin{array}{l} \boldsymbol {\eta} _ {k} ^ {\mathrm {T}}, \boldsymbol {\eta} _ {d} ^ {\mathrm {T}} \end{array} \right] ^ {\mathrm {T}} \tag {4.280}
$$

作为试验模态综合而言，式(4.280)内的 $\pmb{\Phi}_{k}$ 应取其试验测量值。将式(4.280)代入(4.217)并左乘 $\pmb{V}^{\mathrm{T}}$ ，得部件的广义（模态）方程为

$$
A _ {\eta} \dot {\boldsymbol {\eta}} + B _ {\eta} \boldsymbol {\eta} = \boldsymbol {F} _ {\eta} \tag {4.281}
$$

式中

$$
\left\{ \begin{array}{l} \boldsymbol {A} _ {\eta} = \boldsymbol {V} ^ {\mathrm {T}} \boldsymbol {A} \boldsymbol {U} = \operatorname {d i a g} \left[ \overline {{\boldsymbol {A}}} _ {k k}, \overline {{\boldsymbol {A}}} _ {d d} \right], \\ \boldsymbol {B} _ {\eta} = \boldsymbol {V} ^ {\mathrm {T}} \boldsymbol {B} \boldsymbol {U} = \operatorname {d i a g} \left[ \overline {{\boldsymbol {B}}} _ {k k}, \overline {{\boldsymbol {B}}} _ {d d} \right], \\ \overline {{\boldsymbol {A}}} _ {s s} = \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {s} ^ {\mathrm {T}} \boldsymbol {A} \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {s}, \overline {{\boldsymbol {B}}} _ {s s} = \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {s} ^ {\mathrm {T}} \boldsymbol {B} \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {s}, (s = k, d) \\ \boldsymbol {F} _ {\eta} = \boldsymbol {V} ^ {\mathrm {T}} \boldsymbol {F} = \left[ \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {b k} ^ {D}, \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {b d} ^ {D} \right] ^ {\mathrm {T}} f _ {b} \end{array} \right. \tag {4.282}
$$

关于式(4.282)中的 $F_{\eta}$ 表达式，按下列推演便可得知：因为 $\pmb{V}$ 和 $\pmb{F}$ 可以分割成如下：

$$
\boldsymbol {V} = \left[ \begin{array}{l l} \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {k}, \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {d} \end{array} \right] = \left[ \begin{array}{l l} \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {k} ^ {V} & \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {d} ^ {V} \\ \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {k} ^ {D} & \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {d} ^ {D} \end{array} \right] = \left[ \begin{array}{l l} \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {i k} ^ {V} & \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {i d} ^ {V} \\ \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {b k} ^ {V} & \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {b d} ^ {V} \\ \dots \dots \dots \dots \dots \dots \dots \dots \dots \dots \dots \dots \dots \dots \dots \dots \dots \dots \dots \dots \dots \dots \dots \dots \dots \dots \\ \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {i k} ^ {D} & \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {i d} ^ {D} \\ \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {b k} ^ {D} & \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {b d} ^ {D} \end{array} \right]
$$

$$
\boldsymbol {F} = \left[ \begin{array}{l} \boldsymbol {O} \\ \boldsymbol {f} \end{array} \right] = \left[ \begin{array}{l} \boldsymbol {O} \\ \boldsymbol {O} \\ \dots \\ \boldsymbol {O} \\ \boldsymbol {f} _ {b} \end{array} \right]
$$

所以

$$
\boldsymbol {V} ^ {\mathrm {T}} \boldsymbol {F} = \left[ \begin{array}{l l l l} \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {i k} ^ {V T} & \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {b k} ^ {V T} & \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {i k} ^ {D T} & \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {b k} ^ {D T} \\ \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {i d} ^ {V T} & \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {b d} ^ {V T} & \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {i d} ^ {D T} & \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {b d} ^ {D T} \end{array} \right] \left[ \begin{array}{l} \boldsymbol {O} \\ \boldsymbol {O} \\ \boldsymbol {O} \\ f _ {b} \end{array} \right] = \left[ \begin{array}{l} \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {b k} ^ {D T} \\ \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {b d} ^ {D T} \end{array} \right] f _ {b}
$$

为了后述结论的需要，还要证明关于 $\overline{A}_{dd}$ 和 $\overline{B}_{dd}$ 的两个表达式。首先由式(4.222），可以推知

$$
\overline {{A}} _ {h h} \overline {{B}} _ {h h} ^ {- 1} = - A _ {h h} ^ {- 1} \tag {4.283}
$$

于是有

$$
\bar {B} _ {h h} ^ {- 1} = - \bar {A} _ {h h} ^ {- 1} A _ {h h} ^ {- 1} \tag {4.284}
$$

然后将式（4.275a）和式（4.277a）代入式（4.282），且利用式(4.283)及式(4.284），得

$$
\begin{array}{l} \overline {{\boldsymbol {A}}} _ {d d} = \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {d} ^ {\mathrm {T}} \boldsymbol {A} \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {d} = \left(\boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {b h} ^ {D} \overline {{\boldsymbol {B}}} _ {h h} ^ {- 1} \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {h} ^ {\mathrm {T}}\right) \boldsymbol {A} \left(\boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {h} \overline {{\boldsymbol {B}}} _ {h h} ^ {- 1} \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {b h} ^ {D T}\right) \\ = \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {b h} ^ {D} \overline {{\boldsymbol {B}}} _ {h h} ^ {- 1} \overline {{\boldsymbol {A}}} _ {h h} \overline {{\boldsymbol {B}}} _ {h h} ^ {- 1} \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {b h} ^ {D T} = \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {b h} ^ {D} \left(- \overline {{\boldsymbol {A}}} _ {h h} ^ {- 1} \boldsymbol {\Lambda} _ {h h} ^ {- 1}\right) \left(- \boldsymbol {\Lambda} _ {h h} ^ {- 1}\right) \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {b h} ^ {D T} \\ = \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {b h} ^ {D} \overline {{\boldsymbol {A}}} _ {h h} ^ {- 1} \boldsymbol {\Lambda} _ {h h} ^ {- 2} \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {b h} ^ {D T} \tag {4.285} \\ \end{array}
$$

类似可得

$$
\begin{array}{l} \overline {{B}} _ {d d} = \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {d} ^ {D} \boldsymbol {B} \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {d} = \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {b h} ^ {D} \overline {{B}} _ {h h} ^ {- 1} \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {h} ^ {\mathrm {T}} \boldsymbol {B} \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {h} \overline {{B}} _ {h h} ^ {- 1} \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {b h} ^ {D T} \\ = \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {b h} ^ {D} \overline {{\boldsymbol {B}}} _ {h h} ^ {- 1} \overline {{\boldsymbol {B}}} _ {h h} \overline {{\boldsymbol {B}}} _ {h h} ^ {- 1} \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {b h} ^ {D \Gamma} = \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {b h} ^ {D} \overline {{\boldsymbol {B}}} _ {h h} ^ {- 1} \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {b h} ^ {D \Gamma} \\ \end{array}
$$

再利用式(4.275b)和式(4.278)，上式可进一步写成

$$
\overline {{B}} _ {d d} = \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {b h} ^ {D} \overline {{B}} _ {h h} ^ {- 1} \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {b h} ^ {D T} = \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {b d} ^ {D} = \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {b d} ^ {D T} \tag {4.286}
$$

最后将式(4.281)写成分割形式，有

$$
\left[ \begin{array}{l l} \bar {A} _ {k k} & 0 \\ 0 & \bar {A} _ {d d} \end{array} \right] \left[ \begin{array}{l} \dot {\eta} _ {k} \\ \dot {\eta} _ {d} \end{array} \right] + \left[ \begin{array}{l l} \bar {B} _ {k k} & 0 \\ 0 & \bar {B} _ {d d} \end{array} \right] \left[ \begin{array}{l} \eta_ {k} \\ \eta_ {d} \end{array} \right] = \left[ \begin{array}{l} \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {b k} ^ {D T} \\ \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {b d} ^ {D T} \end{array} \right] f _ {b} \tag {4.287}
$$

由式(4.287)的第二行，得

$$
\overline {{A}} _ {d d} \dot {\boldsymbol {\eta}} _ {d} + \overline {{B}} _ {d d} \boldsymbol {\eta} _ {d} = \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {b d} ^ {D T} f _ {b} \tag {4.288}
$$

将式(4.286)引入式(4.288)，便可写出

$$
\bar {A} _ {d d} \dot {\boldsymbol {\eta}} _ {d} + \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {b d} ^ {D} \boldsymbol {\eta} _ {d} = \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {b d} ^ {D} \boldsymbol {f} _ {b} \tag {4.289}
$$

略去 $\dot{\pmb{\eta}}_d$ 影响并注意 $\pmb{\Phi}_{bd}^{D}$ 非奇异，便得到

$$
\boldsymbol {\eta} _ {d} = \boldsymbol {f} _ {b} \tag {4.290}
$$

可见右剩余模态坐标 $\pmb{\eta}_d$ 的伪静态响应近似为界面力 $\pmb{f}_b$ 。对式(4.219)做坐标变换，则

$$
\boldsymbol {Y} = \boldsymbol {V} \boldsymbol {\xi} = \left[ \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {k}, \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {d} \right] \left[ \boldsymbol {\xi} _ {k} ^ {\mathrm {T}}, \boldsymbol {\xi} _ {d} ^ {\mathrm {T}} \right] ^ {\mathrm {T}} \tag {4.291}
$$

则相应可以得到

$$
\boldsymbol {\xi} _ {d} = f _ {b} ^ {*} \tag {4.292}
$$

这说明左剩余模态坐标的伪静态响应近似等于伴随界面力。

# 4. 综合方程[63]

设整体结构被拆分成 $N$ 个部件, 这 $N$ 个部件将分别做自由~自由模态试验。现重写式(4.281)如下

$$
\left(A _ {\eta} \dot {\boldsymbol {\eta}} + B _ {\eta} \boldsymbol {\eta}\right) = ^ {(\alpha)} F _ {\eta} \quad (\alpha = 1, 2, \dots N) \tag {4.293}
$$

左上标 $(\alpha)$ 表示限定量属于第 $\alpha$ 部件, 依次取 $\alpha$ 为1至 $N$ 。将式(4.293)的 $N$ 个方程堆聚为下列总体方程：

$$
A _ {\mu} \dot {\boldsymbol {\mu}} + B _ {\mu} \boldsymbol {\mu} = F _ {\mu} \tag {4.294}
$$

式中

$$
\boldsymbol {A} _ {\mu} = \operatorname {d i a g} \left[ ^ {(\alpha)} \boldsymbol {A} _ {\eta} \right], \boldsymbol {B} _ {\mu} = \operatorname {d i a g} \left[ ^ {(\alpha)} \boldsymbol {B} _ {\eta} \right],
$$

$$
\boldsymbol {\mu} = \operatorname {c o l} \left[ ^ {(\alpha)} \boldsymbol {\eta} \right], \boldsymbol {F} _ {\mu} = \operatorname {c o l} \left[ ^ {(\alpha)} \boldsymbol {F} _ {\eta} \right] \tag {4.295}
$$

令统一编号的独立界面力列向量为 $f_{E}$ 或 $\pmb{\eta}_{E}$ 。某部件界面力 ${}^{(\alpha)}f_{b}$ 与 $f_{E}$ 的关系可以通过指示矩阵 ${}^{(\alpha)}\pmb{E}_{bE}$ 写为

$$
{ } ^ { ( \alpha ) } f _ { b } = { } ^ { ( \alpha ) } E _ { b E } f _ { E } \tag {4.296}
$$

此式实质是部件界面力之间的协调条件，按式（4.290）它又可写为

$$
{ } ^ { ( \alpha ) } \boldsymbol { \eta } _ { d } = { } ^ { ( \alpha ) } E _ { b E } \boldsymbol { \eta } _ { E } \tag {4.297}
$$

总体方程(4.294)的第一次坐标变换为

$$
\boldsymbol {\mu} = S \boldsymbol {\sigma} \tag {4.298}
$$

式中

$$
\left\{ \begin{array}{l} \boldsymbol {\mu} = \operatorname {c o l} \left[ \begin{array}{l} ^ {(\alpha)} \\ & \left[ \begin{array}{l} \boldsymbol {\eta} _ {k} \\ \boldsymbol {\eta} _ {d} \end{array} \right] \end{array} \right], \boldsymbol {\sigma} = \left[ \begin{array}{l} z \\ \boldsymbol {\eta} _ {E} \end{array} \right], \\ S = \operatorname {c o l} [ ^ {(\alpha)} S ], z = \operatorname {c o l} [ ^ {(\alpha)} \boldsymbol {\eta} _ {k} ] \\ ^ {(\alpha)} S = \left[ \begin{array}{l l l l} O \dots O & ^ {(\alpha)} I _ {k k} & O \dots O & O \\ O \dots O & O & O \dots O & ^ {(\alpha)} E _ {b E} \end{array} \right] \end{array} \right. \tag {4.299}
$$

将式(4.298)代入式(4.294)，并左乘 $S^{\top}$ ，得

$$
A _ {\sigma} \dot {\boldsymbol {\sigma}} + B _ {\sigma} \boldsymbol {\sigma} = F _ {\sigma} \tag {4.300}
$$

式中

$$
\left\{ \begin{array}{l} \boldsymbol {A} _ {\sigma} = \boldsymbol {S} ^ {\mathrm {T}} \boldsymbol {A} _ {\mu} \boldsymbol {S} = \sum_ {\alpha = 1} ^ {N} ^ {(\alpha)} (\boldsymbol {S} ^ {\mathrm {T}} \boldsymbol {A} _ {\eta} \boldsymbol {S}) = \operatorname {d i a g} [ \overline {{\boldsymbol {A}}} _ {L L}, \overline {{\boldsymbol {A}}} _ {E E} ] \\ \boldsymbol {B} _ {\sigma} = \operatorname {d i a g} [ \overline {{\boldsymbol {B}}} _ {L L}, \overline {{\boldsymbol {B}}} _ {E E} ] \end{array} \right. \tag {4.301}
$$

$$
\left\{ \begin{array}{l} A _ {L L} = \operatorname {d i a g} \left[ ^ {(\alpha)} \overline {{A}} _ {k k} \right], \overline {{A}} _ {E E} = \sum_ {\alpha = 1} ^ {N} ^ {(\alpha)} \left(E _ {b E} ^ {\mathrm {T}} \overline {{A}} _ {d d} E _ {b E}\right) \\ \overline {{B}} _ {L L} = \operatorname {d i a g} \left[ ^ {(\alpha)} \overline {{B}} _ {k k} \right], \overline {{B}} _ {E E} = \sum_ {\alpha = 1} ^ {N} ^ {(\alpha)} \left(E _ {b E} ^ {\mathrm {T}} \overline {{B}} _ {d d} E _ {b E}\right) \end{array} \right. \tag {4.302}
$$

式(4.300)的右端项为

$$
\boldsymbol {F} _ {\sigma} = \boldsymbol {S} ^ {\mathrm {T}} \boldsymbol {F} _ {\mu} = \sum_ {\alpha = 1} ^ {N} ^ {(\alpha)} \left(\boldsymbol {S} ^ {\mathrm {T}} \boldsymbol {F} _ {\eta}\right) = \left[ \boldsymbol {R} _ {E L}, \boldsymbol {R} _ {E E} \right] ^ {\mathrm {T}} \boldsymbol {f} _ {E} \tag {4.303}
$$

式中

$$
\boldsymbol {R} _ {\mathcal {E L}} = \operatorname {r o w} \left[ ^ {(\alpha)} \left(\boldsymbol {E} _ {b E} ^ {\mathrm {T}} \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {b d} ^ {D}\right) \right], \boldsymbol {R} _ {E E} = \sum_ {\alpha = 1} ^ {N} ^ {(\alpha)} \left(\boldsymbol {E} _ {b E} ^ {\mathrm {T}} \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {b d} ^ {D} \boldsymbol {E} _ {b E}\right) \tag {4.304}
$$

现基于式(4.286)来比较式(4.302)和式(4.304)，可得

$$
\boldsymbol {R} _ {E E} ^ {\top} = \overline {{\boldsymbol {B}}} _ {E E} \tag {4.305}
$$

将式(4.280)按式(4.274)进行分块，有

$$
\left\{ \begin{array}{l} x _ {i} ^ {V} \\ x _ {b} ^ {V} \\ x _ {i} ^ {D} \\ x _ {b} ^ {D} \end{array} \right\} = \left[ \begin{array}{c} \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {i k} ^ {V} \\ \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {b k} ^ {V} \\ \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {i k} ^ {D} \\ \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {b k} ^ {D} \end{array} \right] \quad \left( \begin{array}{l} \alpha \\ \alpha \end{array} \right) \boldsymbol {\eta} _ {k} + \left[ \begin{array}{c} \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {i d} ^ {V} \\ \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {b d} ^ {V} \\ \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {i d} ^ {D} \\ \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {b d} ^ {D} \end{array} \right] \quad \left( \begin{array}{l} \alpha \\ \alpha \end{array} \right) \boldsymbol {\eta} _ {d}
$$

由上式第四行，得

$$
{ } ^ { ( \alpha ) } x _ { b } = { } ^ { ( \alpha ) } \left( \boldsymbol { \Phi } _ { b k } ^ { D } \boldsymbol { \eta } _ { k } + \boldsymbol { \Phi } _ { b d } ^ { D } \boldsymbol { \eta } _ { d } \right) \tag {4.306}
$$

这里已将 $x_{b}^{D}$ 写成 $\pmb{x}_{b}$ 了。将式(4.297)代入式(4.306)，并左乘以 $(^{\alpha})\dot{E}_{bE}^{\mathrm{T}}$ ，然后依次取 $\alpha$ 为1至 $N$ 进行累加，得

$$
\sum_ {\alpha = 1} ^ {N} ^ {(\alpha)} \left(E _ {b E} ^ {T} x _ {b}\right) = \sum_ {\alpha = 1} ^ {N} ^ {(\alpha)} \left(E _ {b E} ^ {T} \Phi_ {b k} ^ {D} \eta_ {k}\right) + \sum_ {\alpha = 1} ^ {N} ^ {(\alpha)} \left(E _ {b E} ^ {T} \Phi_ {b d} ^ {D} E _ {b E}\right) \eta_ {E} \tag {4.307}
$$

对于具有正常界面的邻接部件, 式(4.296)内的 $E_{bE}$ 已反映了界面力以作用力与反作用力成对出现的性质, 故而当邻接部件在界面

上保持位移协调时，必有

$$
\sum_ {\alpha = 1} ^ {N} ^ {(\alpha)} \left(\boldsymbol {E} _ {b E} ^ {T} \boldsymbol {x} _ {b}\right) = O \tag {4.308}
$$

此式实质为部件界面位移协调条件。这样，由式(4.307)便可解出

$$
\boldsymbol {\eta} _ {E} = - \boldsymbol {H} _ {E E} ^ {- 1} \boldsymbol {H} _ {E L} z \tag {4.309}
$$

式中

$$
\boldsymbol {H} _ {E L} = \operatorname {r o w} \left[ ^ {(\alpha)} \left(\boldsymbol {E} _ {b E} ^ {\mathrm {T}} \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {b k} ^ {D}\right) \right], \boldsymbol {H} _ {E E} = \sum_ {\alpha = 1} ^ {N} ^ {(\alpha)} \left(\boldsymbol {E} _ {b E} ^ {\mathrm {T}} \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {b d} ^ {D} \boldsymbol {E} _ {b E}\right) \tag {4.310}
$$

关于 $z$ 的定义请见式(4.299)。基于式(4.286)，由式(4.302）、式(4.304）和式(4.305），可得

$$
\boldsymbol {H} _ {E E} = \overline {{\boldsymbol {B}}} _ {E E} = \boldsymbol {R} _ {E E} ^ {\mathrm {T}} \tag {4.311}
$$

若将独立的伴随界面力也按 $f_{E}$ 的排列方式统一编号就可得到 $\pmb{f}_{E}^{*}$ , 于是有

$$
\stackrel {(\alpha)} {f} _ {b} ^ {*} = \stackrel {(\dot {a})} {E} E _ {b E} f _ {E} ^ {*} \tag {4.312}
$$

或写为

$$
\left(^ {(\alpha)} \xi_ {d} = ^ {(\alpha)} E _ {b E} \xi_ {E} \right. \tag {4.313}
$$

经过前述类似过程可以推得

$$
\boldsymbol {\xi} _ {E} = - \boldsymbol {R} _ {E E} ^ {- 1} \boldsymbol {R} _ {E L} \boldsymbol {w} \tag {4.314}
$$

式中

$$
w = \operatorname {c o l} \left[ ^ {(\alpha)} \xi_ {k} \right] \tag {4.315}
$$

根据式(4.309)可以建立总体方程的第二次坐标变换为

$$
\boldsymbol {\sigma} = \boldsymbol {H z} \tag {4.316}
$$

式中

$$
\boldsymbol {H} = \left[ \begin{array}{c} \boldsymbol {I} _ {U L} \\ - \boldsymbol {H} _ {E E} ^ {- 1} \boldsymbol {H} _ {E L} \end{array} \right], \boldsymbol {I} _ {U L} = \operatorname {d i a g} \left[ \begin{array}{l} (\alpha) \boldsymbol {I} _ {k k} \end{array} \right] \tag {4.317}
$$

注意：式(4.316)右端的独立坐标 $\pmb{z}$ 中已消除了全部剩余模态坐标 ${}^{(\alpha)}\pmb{\eta}_d$ 。再令

$$
\boldsymbol {R} = \left[ \begin{array}{c} \boldsymbol {I} _ {L L} \\ - \boldsymbol {R} _ {E E} ^ {- 1} \boldsymbol {R} _ {E L} \end{array} \right] \tag {4.318}
$$

现将式(4.316)代入式(4.300)，且左乘以 $\pmb{R}^{\mathrm{T}}$ 和注意到式(4.311)就得到最终的综合方程为

$$
A _ {z} \dot {z} + B _ {z} z = 0 \tag {4.319}
$$

式中

$$
\begin{array}{l} \boldsymbol {A} _ {z} = \boldsymbol {R} ^ {\mathrm {T}} \boldsymbol {A} _ {\sigma} \boldsymbol {R} = \bar {\boldsymbol {A}} _ {\mathcal {L L}} + \boldsymbol {R} _ {\boldsymbol {E L}} ^ {\mathrm {T}} \boldsymbol {R} _ {\boldsymbol {E E}} ^ {- \mathrm {T}} \bar {\boldsymbol {A}} _ {\boldsymbol {E E}} \boldsymbol {H} _ {\boldsymbol {E E}} ^ {- 1} \boldsymbol {H} _ {\boldsymbol {E L}} \\ = \bar {A} _ {L L} + R _ {E L} ^ {\mathrm {T}} \left(H _ {E E} ^ {- 1} \bar {A} _ {E E} H _ {E E} ^ {- 1}\right) H _ {E L} \tag {4.320a} \\ \end{array}
$$

$$
\begin{array}{l} \boldsymbol {B} _ {z} = \boldsymbol {R} ^ {\mathsf {T}} \boldsymbol {B} _ {\sigma} \boldsymbol {R} = \bar {\boldsymbol {B}} _ {L L} + \boldsymbol {R} _ {E L} ^ {\mathsf {T}} \boldsymbol {R} _ {E E} ^ {- \mathsf {T}} \bar {\boldsymbol {B}} _ {E E} \boldsymbol {H} _ {E E} ^ {- 1} \boldsymbol {H} _ {E L} \\ = \bar {\boldsymbol {B}} _ {U L} + \boldsymbol {R} _ {E L} ^ {T} \boldsymbol {H} _ {E E} ^ {- 1} \boldsymbol {H} _ {E L} \tag {4.320b} \\ \end{array}
$$

式(4.319)的右端 $R^{\mathrm{T}}F_{\sigma} = 0$ 。

式(4.319)的特征值问题为

$$
\left(\lambda A _ {z} + B _ {z}\right) z = O \tag {4.321}
$$

求解式(4.321)便可得整体结构的前若干阶复特征值 $\lambda$ 。另外, 将相应的复特征向量 $z$ 组成的矩阵记为 $Z$ , 则整体结构在原物理坐标空间内的复模态为

$$
X _ {g} = T _ {g} Z \tag {4.322}
$$

式中

$$
X _ {g} = \operatorname {c o l} [ ^ {(\alpha)} x ] \tag {4.323a}
$$

$$
\boldsymbol {T} _ {\mathbf {g}} = \operatorname {d i a g} \left[ ^ {(a)} \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {k} ^ {D} \right] - \operatorname {c o l} \left[ ^ {(a)} \left(\boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {d} ^ {D} \boldsymbol {E} _ {b E}\right) \right] \boldsymbol {H} _ {E E} ^ {- 1} \operatorname {r o w} \left[ ^ {(a)} \left(\boldsymbol {E} _ {b E} ^ {\mathrm {T}} \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {b k} ^ {D}\right) \right] \tag {4.323b}
$$

注意：这里的 $T_{g}$ 矩阵相当于由三级坐标变换阵 $U, S, H$ 连乘（回代）得到的。本节方法属于前述“试验/理论模态基”综合技术。

# 4.4.3 实空间解耦模态综合法[60]

对于不考虑阻尼的线性振动系统模态综合方法，由于子结构系统在其模态空间满足正交性，因此动力学方程在模态空间可以解耦，使得综合的表达式大大简化。对于带有粘滞阻尼的线性振动系统，阻尼矩阵对于无阻尼模态空间可以不满足正交性，这样就会导致动力学方程在模态空间不能解耦。为了能够解耦，需要将带有粘滞阻尼的动力学方程写成状态方程的形式，这样对应的模态空间将是复模态空间，而复模态空间是不利于进行模态综合的。为此，本节方法通过对复模态空间合成，组合出一个新的实模态空间，将子结构的物理位移在新的实模态空间进行分解，从而推导出针对带有粘滞阻尼的线性系统的模态综合方法。

# 1. 基于实矩阵的模态变换

带有粘滞阻尼的离散振动系统运动方程为二阶常微分方程组，即

$$
M \ddot {u} + C \dot {u} + K u = f \tag {4.324}
$$

式中： $M, C, K$ 分别为 $n$ 阶的质量矩阵，阻尼矩阵和刚度矩阵，可以是不对称的。 $\pmb{u}$ 和 $\pmb{f}$ 分别是广义位移向量和载荷向量。式(4.324)变换到状态空间，有

$$
\boldsymbol {A} \dot {\boldsymbol {x}} + \boldsymbol {B} \boldsymbol {x} = \boldsymbol {F} \tag {4.325}
$$

式中

$$
A = \left[ \begin{array}{l l} C & M \\ M & 0 \end{array} \right] \quad B = \left[ \begin{array}{c c} K & 0 \\ 0 & - M \end{array} \right] \quad x = \left\{ \begin{array}{l l} u \\ \dot {u} \end{array} \right\} \quad F = \left\{ \begin{array}{l} f \\ 0 \end{array} \right\} \tag {4.326}
$$

设 $s_j, y_j, z_j$ 为系统的第 $j$ 阶复特征对，其中 $s_j$ 为第 $j$ 阶复特征值， $y_j$ 为第 $j$ 阶右复特征向量， $z_j$ 为第 $j$ 阶左复特征向量， $\bar{s}_j, \bar{y}_j, \bar{z}_j$ 是其相应的共轭复特征对。设

$$
S = \left[ \begin{array}{c c c c} s _ {1} & & & \\ & s _ {2} & & \\ & & \ddots & \\ & & & s _ {n} \end{array} \right], \bar {S} = \left[ \begin{array}{c c c c} \bar {s} _ {1} & & & \\ & \bar {s} _ {2} & & \\ & & \ddots & \\ & & & \bar {s} _ {n} \end{array} \right] \tag {4.327a}
$$

$$
\begin{array}{l} Y = \left[ \begin{array}{l l l l} y _ {1} & y _ {2} & \dots & y _ {n} \end{array} \right], \quad \bar {Y} = \left[ \begin{array}{l l l l} \bar {y} _ {1} & \bar {y} _ {2} & \dots & \bar {y} _ {n} \end{array} \right] (4.327b) \\ Z = \left[ \begin{array}{l l l l} z _ {1} & z _ {2} & \dots & z _ {n} \end{array} \right], \quad \bar {Z} = \left[ \begin{array}{l l l l} \bar {z} _ {1} & \bar {z} _ {2} & \dots & \bar {z} _ {n} \end{array} \right] (4.327c) \\ \end{array}
$$

式中： $S, Y, Z$ 为系统的复特征对的完备矩阵， $\overline{S}, \overline{Y}, \overline{Z}$ 为其共轭矩阵（本节都用顶符 - 表示共轭）。在 $Y, Z$ 对 $A$ 矩阵进行归一化后，有

$$
\begin{array}{l} \left[ \begin{array}{c c} Z & \bar {Z} \end{array} \right] ^ {\mathsf {T}} A \left[ \begin{array}{c c} Y & \bar {Y} \end{array} \right] = \left[ \begin{array}{c c} I & 0 \\ 0 & I \end{array} \right], \\ \left[ \begin{array}{l l} \boldsymbol {Z} & \bar {\boldsymbol {Z}} \end{array} \right] ^ {\intercal} \boldsymbol {B} \left[ \begin{array}{l l} \boldsymbol {Y} & \bar {\boldsymbol {Y}} \end{array} \right] = \left[ \begin{array}{c c} - \boldsymbol {S} & 0 \\ 0 & - \bar {\boldsymbol {S}} \end{array} \right] \tag {4.328} \\ \end{array}
$$

如果按照复模态解耦, 将得到 $2n$ 个独立的复系数方程。而我们所希望的是在实空间的解耦, 并希望能够得到与方程(4.325)形式类似的解耦方程, 这样就能还原到类似方程(4.324)的时域方程。试图寻找一个实特征向量基底, 设该基底由以下实特征向量矩阵组成, 即

$$
[ \boldsymbol {\Phi} ] = [ \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {1} \quad \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {2} ], [ \boldsymbol {\Psi} ] = [ \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {1} \quad \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {2} ] \tag {4.329}
$$

$[\Phi], [\Psi]$ 分别为右、左实特征向量矩阵，为 $2n \times 2n$ 阶矩阵， $\Phi_1, \Phi_2, \Psi_1, \Psi_2$ 为 $2n \times n$ 阶矩阵，因此有，

$$
\begin{array}{l} \left[ \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {1} \right] = \left[ \begin{array}{l l l l} \boldsymbol {\phi} _ {1 1} & \boldsymbol {\phi} _ {1 2} & \dots & \boldsymbol {\phi} _ {1 n} \end{array} \right], \left[ \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {2} \right] = \left[ \begin{array}{l l l l} \boldsymbol {\phi} _ {2 1} & \boldsymbol {\phi} _ {2 2} & \dots & \boldsymbol {\phi} _ {2 n} \end{array} \right] (4.330a) \\ \left[ \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {1} \right] = \left[ \begin{array}{l l l l} \boldsymbol {\psi} _ {1 1} & \boldsymbol {\psi} _ {1 2} & \dots & \boldsymbol {\psi} _ {1 n} \end{array} \right], \left[ \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {2} \right] = \left[ \begin{array}{l l l l} \boldsymbol {\psi} _ {2 1} & \boldsymbol {\psi} _ {2 2} & \dots & \boldsymbol {\psi} _ {2 n} \end{array} \right] (4.330b) \\ \end{array}
$$

式中

$$
\left[ \begin{array}{l l} \boldsymbol {\phi} _ {1 i} & \boldsymbol {\phi} _ {2 i} \end{array} \right], \quad \left[ \begin{array}{l l} \boldsymbol {\psi} _ {1 i} & \boldsymbol {\psi} _ {2 i} \end{array} \right] \quad (i = 1, 2, \dots , n) \tag {4.331}
$$

分别为第 $i$ 阶右、左实特征向量。

将每一阶实特征向量表达为复特征向量的线性组合, 则有

$$
\left[ \begin{array}{l l} \boldsymbol {\phi} _ {1 i} & \boldsymbol {\phi} _ {2 i} \end{array} \right] = \left[ \begin{array}{l l} \boldsymbol {y} _ {i} & \bar {\boldsymbol {y}} _ {i} \end{array} \right] \left[ \begin{array}{l l} \alpha_ {1 1} & \alpha_ {1 2} \\ \alpha_ {2 1} & \alpha_ {2 2} \end{array} \right] (i = 1, 2, \dots , n) \tag {4.332a}
$$

$$
\left[ \begin{array}{l l} \boldsymbol {\psi} _ {1 i} & \boldsymbol {\psi} _ {2 i} \end{array} \right] = \left[ \begin{array}{l l} z _ {i} & \bar {z} _ {i} \end{array} \right] \left[ \begin{array}{l l} \alpha_ {1 1} & \alpha_ {1 2} \\ \alpha_ {2 1} & \alpha_ {2 2} \end{array} \right] (i = 1, 2, \dots , n) \tag {4.332b}
$$

为了满足以上两式左端为实特征向量，只需要满足

$$
\alpha_ {2 1} = \bar {\alpha} _ {1 1}, \quad \alpha_ {1 2} = \bar {\alpha} _ {2 2} \tag {4.333}
$$

因此式(4.332)可写成

$$
\left[ \begin{array}{l l} \boldsymbol {\phi} _ {1 i} & \boldsymbol {\phi} _ {2 i} \end{array} \right] = \left[ \begin{array}{l l} \boldsymbol {y} _ {i} & \bar {\boldsymbol {y}} _ {i} \end{array} \right] \left[ \begin{array}{c c} \alpha_ {1 1} & \overline {{\alpha}} _ {2 2} \\ \overline {{\alpha}} _ {1 1} & \alpha_ {2 2} \end{array} \right] (i = 1, 2, \dots , n) \tag {4.334a}
$$

$$
\left[ \begin{array}{l l} \boldsymbol {\psi} _ {1 i} & \boldsymbol {\psi} _ {2 i} \end{array} \right] = \left[ \begin{array}{l l} z _ {i} & \bar {z} _ {i} \end{array} \right] \left[ \begin{array}{l l} \alpha_ {1 1} & \overline {{\alpha}} _ {2 2} \\ \overline {{\alpha}} _ {1 1} & \alpha_ {2 2} \end{array} \right] (i = 1, 2, \dots , n) \tag {4.334b}
$$

当 $i \neq j$ 时要求

$$
\left[ \begin{array}{l l} \boldsymbol {\psi} _ {1 j} & \boldsymbol {\psi} _ {2 j} \end{array} \right] ^ {\mathsf {T}} \boldsymbol {A} \left[ \begin{array}{l l} \boldsymbol {\phi} _ {1 i} & \boldsymbol {\phi} _ {2 i} \end{array} \right] = 0,
$$

$$
\left[ \begin{array}{l l} \boldsymbol {\psi} _ {1 j} & \boldsymbol {\psi} _ {2 j} \end{array} \right] ^ {\mathsf {T}} \boldsymbol {B} \left[ \begin{array}{l l} \boldsymbol {\phi} _ {1 i} & \boldsymbol {\phi} _ {2 i} \end{array} \right] = 0, \tag {4.335}
$$

另外，由式(4.328)，可知

$$
\left[ \begin{array}{l l} z _ {i} & \bar {z} _ {i} \end{array} \right] ^ {\mathsf {T}} A \left[ \begin{array}{l l} y _ {i} & \bar {y} _ {i} \end{array} \right] = \left[ \begin{array}{l l} 1 & 0 \\ 0 & 1 \end{array} \right],
$$

$$
\left[ \begin{array}{l l} z _ {i} & \bar {z} _ {i} \end{array} \right] ^ {\intercal} \boldsymbol {B} \left[ \begin{array}{l l} y _ {i} & \bar {y} _ {i} \end{array} \right] = \left[ \begin{array}{c c} - s _ {i} & 0 \\ 0 & - s _ {i} \end{array} \right] \tag {4.336}
$$

这样，将式(4.334)代入下式，且利用式(4.336），得

$$
\begin{array}{l} \left[ \begin{array}{l l} \boldsymbol {\psi} _ {1 i} & \boldsymbol {\psi} _ {2 i} \end{array} \right] ^ {\mathrm {T}} \boldsymbol {A} \left[ \begin{array}{l l} \boldsymbol {\phi} _ {1 i} & \boldsymbol {\phi} _ {2 i} \end{array} \right] = \left[ \begin{array}{l l} \alpha_ {1 1} & \overline {{\alpha}} _ {2 2} \\ \overline {{\alpha}} _ {1 1} & \alpha_ {2 2} \end{array} \right] ^ {\mathrm {T}} \left[ \begin{array}{l l} \alpha_ {1 1} & \overline {{\alpha}} _ {2 2} \\ \overline {{\alpha}} _ {1 1} & \alpha_ {2 2} \end{array} \right] \\ = \left[ \begin{array}{c c} \alpha_ {1 1} ^ {2} + \bar {\alpha} _ {1 1} ^ {2} & \alpha_ {1 1} \bar {\alpha} _ {2 2} + \bar {\alpha} _ {1 1} \alpha_ {2 2} \\ \alpha_ {1 1} \bar {\alpha} _ {2 2} + \bar {\alpha} _ {1 1} \alpha_ {2 2} & \bar {\alpha} _ {2 2} ^ {2} + \alpha_ {2 2} ^ {2} \end{array} \right] \tag {4.337a} \\ \end{array}
$$

$$
\begin{array}{l} \left[ \begin{array}{l l} \boldsymbol {\psi} _ {1 i} & \boldsymbol {\psi} _ {2 i} \end{array} \right] ^ {\mathrm {T}} \boldsymbol {B} \left[ \begin{array}{l l} \boldsymbol {\phi} _ {1 i} & \boldsymbol {\phi} _ {2 i} \end{array} \right] \\ = \left[ \begin{array}{l l} \alpha_ {1 1} & \bar {\alpha} _ {2 2} \\ \bar {\alpha} _ {1 1} & \alpha_ {2 2} \end{array} \right] ^ {T} \left[ \begin{array}{c c} - s _ {i} & 0 \\ 0 & - \bar {s} _ {i} \end{array} \right] \left[ \begin{array}{l l} \alpha_ {1 1} & \bar {\alpha} _ {2 2} \\ \bar {\alpha} _ {1 1} & \alpha_ {2 2} \end{array} \right] \\ = \left[ \begin{array}{c c} - s _ {i} \alpha_ {1 1} ^ {2} - \bar {s} _ {i} \bar {\alpha} _ {1 1} ^ {2} & - s _ {i} \alpha_ {1 1} \bar {\alpha} _ {2 2} - \bar {s} _ {i} \bar {\alpha} _ {1 1} \alpha_ {2 2} \\ - s _ {i} \alpha_ {1 1} \bar {\alpha} _ {2 2} - \bar {s} _ {i} \bar {\alpha} _ {1 1} \alpha_ {2 2} & - s _ {i} \bar {\alpha} _ {2 2} ^ {2} - \bar {s} _ {i} \alpha_ {2 2} ^ {2} \end{array} \right] \tag {4.337b} \\ \end{array}
$$

现要求式(4.337)的右边具有如下形式：

$$
\left[ \begin{array}{l l} \boldsymbol {\psi} _ {1 i} & \boldsymbol {\psi} _ {2 i} \end{array} \right] ^ {\mathrm {T}} \boldsymbol {A} \left[ \begin{array}{l l} \boldsymbol {\phi} _ {1 i} & \boldsymbol {\phi} _ {2 i} \end{array} \right] = \left[ \begin{array}{c c c} \alpha_ {1 1} ^ {2} + \bar {\alpha} _ {1 1} ^ {- 2} & 1 \\ 1 & 0 \end{array} \right] \tag {4.338a}
$$

$$
\left[ \begin{array}{l l} \boldsymbol {\psi} _ {1 i} & \boldsymbol {\psi} _ {2 i} \end{array} \right] ^ {\mathrm {T}} \boldsymbol {B} \left[ \begin{array}{l l} \boldsymbol {\phi} _ {1 i} & \boldsymbol {\phi} _ {2 i} \end{array} \right] = \left[ \begin{array}{c c} - s _ {i} \alpha_ {1 1} ^ {2} - \bar {s} _ {i} \overline {{\alpha}} _ {1 1} ^ {- 2} & 0 \\ 0 & - 1 \end{array} \right] \tag {4.338b}
$$

因此可以列出如下方程组：

$$
\left\{ \begin{array}{l} \alpha_ {1 1} \bar {\alpha} _ {2 2} + \bar {\alpha} _ {1 1} a _ {2 2} = 1 \\ \bar {\alpha} _ {2 2} ^ {2} + \alpha_ {2 2} ^ {2} = 0 \\ - s _ {i} \alpha_ {1 1} \bar {\alpha} _ {2 2} - \bar {s} _ {i} \bar {\alpha} _ {1 1} \alpha_ {2 2} = 0 \\ - s _ {i} \bar {\alpha} _ {2 2} ^ {2} - \bar {s} _ {i} \alpha_ {2 2} ^ {2} = - 1 \end{array} \right. \tag {4.339}
$$

求解式(4.339)，得

$$
\left\{ \begin{array}{l} \alpha_ {1 1} = \pm s _ {i} \left(\bar {s} _ {i} - s _ {i}\right) ^ {- \frac {1}{2}} \\ \alpha_ {2 2} = \mp \left(\bar {s} _ {i} - s _ {i}\right) ^ {- \frac {1}{2}} \end{array} \right. \tag {4.340}
$$

根据式(4.327)，可以将式(4.340)写成如下矩阵形式，有

$$
\boldsymbol {H} = \left[ \begin{array}{l l} \boldsymbol {H} _ {1 1} & \overline {{\boldsymbol {H}}} _ {2 2} \\ \overline {{\boldsymbol {H}}} _ {1 1} & \boldsymbol {H} _ {2 2} \end{array} \right] \tag {4.341}
$$

式中

$$
\left\{ \begin{array}{l} \boldsymbol {H} _ {1 1} = \pm (\boldsymbol {S} - \bar {\boldsymbol {S}}) ^ {- \frac {1}{2}} \bar {\boldsymbol {S}} \\ \bar {\boldsymbol {H}} _ {1 1} = \pm (\bar {\boldsymbol {S}} - \boldsymbol {S}) ^ {- \frac {1}{2}} \boldsymbol {S} \\ \boldsymbol {H} _ {2 2} = \mp (\bar {\boldsymbol {S}} - \boldsymbol {S}) ^ {- \frac {1}{2}} \\ \bar {\boldsymbol {H}} _ {2 2} = \mp (\boldsymbol {S} - \bar {\boldsymbol {S}}) ^ {- \frac {1}{2}} \end{array} \right. \tag {4.342}
$$

由式(4.332)，可知

$$
\left[ \begin{array}{l l} \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {1} & \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {2} \end{array} \right] = \left[ \begin{array}{l l} \boldsymbol {Y} & \overline {{\boldsymbol {Y}}} \end{array} \right] \boldsymbol {H} & \left[ \begin{array}{l l} \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {1} & \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {2} \end{array} \right] = \left[ \begin{array}{l l} \boldsymbol {Z} & \overline {{\boldsymbol {Z}}} \end{array} \right] \boldsymbol {H} \tag {4.343}
$$

根据式(4.338)和利用式(4.340)，便得

$$
\left[ \begin{array}{l l} \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {1} & \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {2} \end{array} \right] ^ {\mathrm {T}} \boldsymbol {A} \left[ \begin{array}{l l} \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {1} & \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {2} \end{array} \right] = \left[ \begin{array}{c c} - S - \bar {S} & I \\ I & 0 \end{array} \right] \tag {4.344a}
$$

$$
\left[ \begin{array}{l l} \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {1} & \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {2} \end{array} \right] ^ {\mathrm {T}} \boldsymbol {B} \left[ \begin{array}{l l} \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {1} & \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {2} \end{array} \right] = \left[ \begin{array}{c c} \bar {S S} & 0 \\ 0 & - I \end{array} \right] \tag {4.344b}
$$

这样就找到了一组实振型基底 $[\pmb{\Phi}]$ 、 $[\pmb{\Psi}]$ ，该基底对状态矩阵满足式(4.344)的正交性。

# 2. 系统方程的实空间解耦

引入新的模态变换

$$
\boldsymbol {x} = \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {1} \boldsymbol {q} + \boldsymbol {\Phi} _ {2} \boldsymbol {p} \tag {4.345}
$$

注意到上式中所有的量都为实的。将式(4.345)代入式(4.325)，前乘 $\left[\begin{array}{cc}\boldsymbol{\Psi}_1 & \boldsymbol{\Psi}_2\end{array}\right]^{\mathrm{T}}$ ，根据加权正交关系式(4.344)，可得

$$
\left[ \begin{array}{c c} - S - \bar {S} & I \\ I & O \end{array} \right] \left\{ \begin{array}{l} \dot {\boldsymbol {q}} \\ \dot {\boldsymbol {p}} \end{array} \right\} + \left[ \begin{array}{c c} S \bar {S} & O \\ O & - I \end{array} \right] \left\{ \begin{array}{l} \boldsymbol {q} \\ \boldsymbol {p} \end{array} \right\} = \left\{ \begin{array}{l l} \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {1} ^ {\mathrm {T}} & \boldsymbol {F} \\ \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {2} ^ {\mathrm {T}} & \boldsymbol {F} \end{array} \right\} \tag {4.346}
$$

从这一方程的下半部分，可得

$$
\boldsymbol {p} = \boldsymbol {q} - \boldsymbol {\Psi} _ {2} ^ {\mathrm {T}} \boldsymbol {F} \tag {4.347}
$$

代回到方程的上半部分, 得到系统解耦后的二阶方程为

$$
